śrīgaṇādhipataye namaḥ 
sarasvatyainamaḥ 
atha śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇaṃ prārabhyate 
tatrādau karmakāṇḍākhyaḥ pūrvakhaṇḍaḥ prārabhyate 
oṃ nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam 
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayamudīrayet  GarPMang 
oṃ ajamajaramanantaṃ jñānarūpaṃ mahāntaṃ śivamamalamanādiṃ bhūtadehādihīnam

 nanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargo hi sa smṛtaḥ  GarP

 tadūrdhvastotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ 
 tator'vāksrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mā nuṣaḥ  GarP

sthāvarāntāḥ surādyāstu prajā rudra 
caturvidhāḥ  GarP

etān grāmyānpaśūnprāhurāraṇyāṃśca nibodha me 
śvāpadaṃ dvikhuraṃ hastivānarāḥ pakṣipañcamāḥ  GarP

brahmacārivratasthānāṃ brahmalokaḥ prajāyate

etatstotraṃ japetpaścātsarvavyādhivināśanam 
namaḥ sudarśanāyaiva sahasrādityavarcase  GarP 
jvālāmālāpradīptāya sahasrārāya cakṣuṣe 
sarvaduṣṭavināśāya sarvapātakamardine  GarP 
sucakrāya vicakrāya sarvamantravibhedine 
prasavitre jagaddhātre jagadvidhvaṃsine namaḥ  GarP 
pālanārthāya lokānāṃ duṣṭāsuravināśine 
ugrāya caiva saumyāya caṇḍāya ca namonamaḥ  GarP 
namaścakṣuḥ kvarūpāya saṃsārabhayabhedine 
māyāpañjarabhetre ca śivāya ca namonamaḥ  GarP 
grahātigraharūpāya grahāṇāṃ pateya namaḥ 
kālāya mṛtyave caiva bhīmāya ca namonamaḥ  GarP 
bhaktānugrahadātre ca bhaktagoptre namonamaḥ 
viṣṇurūpāya śāntāya cāyudhānāṃ dharāya ca  GarP 
viṣṇuśastrāya cakrāya namo bhūyo namonamaḥ 
iti stotraṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ cakrasya tava kīrtitam  GarP 
yaḥ paṭhetparayā bhaktyā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati 
cakrapūjāvidhiṃ yaśca paṭhedrudra jitondriyaḥ 
sa pāpaṃ bhasmasātkṛtvā viṣṇulokāya kalpate  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe sudarśanapūjāvidhirnāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
rudra uvāca 
punardevārcanaṃ brūhi hṛṣīkeśa gadādhara 
śṛṇvato nāsti tṛptirme gadatastava pūjanam  GarP 
hariruvāca 
hayagrīvasya devasya pūjanaṃ kathayāmi te 
tacchṛṇuṣva jagannātho yena viṣṇuḥ pratuṣyati  GarP 
mūlamantraṃ mahādeva hayagrīvasya vācakam 
pravakṣyāmi paraṃ puṇyaṃ tadādau śṛṇu śaṅkara  GarP 
oṃ saiṃ kṣaiṃ śirase namaḥ iti praṇavasaṃyutaḥ 
ayaṃ navākṣaromantraḥ sarvavidyāpradāyakaḥ  GarP 
asyāṅgāni mahādeva tāñchṛṇuṣva vṛṣadhvaja 
oṃ kṣāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ 
oṃ kṣīṃ śirase svāhāśiraḥ proktaṃ kṣūṃ vaṣaṭ tathā  GarP 
oṃ kārayuktā devasya śikhā jñeyā vṛṣadhvaja 
oṃ kṣaiṃ kavacāya huṃ vai kavacaṃ parikīrtitam  GarP 
oṃ kṣaiṃ netratrayāya vauṣaṭ netraṃ devasya kīrtitam 
oṃ haḥ astrāya phaṭ astraṃ devasya kīrtitam  GarP 
pūjāvidhiṃ pravakṣyāmi nanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu ādau snātvā tathācamya tato yāgagṛhaṃ vrajet  GarP 
tataḥ praviśya vidhivatkuryādvaṃ śoṣaṇādikam 
yaṃ kṣaiṃ ramiti bījaiśca kaṭhinīkṛtya lamiti  GarP 
aṇḍamutpādya ca tataḥ oṃ kāreṇaiva bhedayet 
aṇḍamadhye hayagrīvamātmānaṃ paricintayet  GarP 
śaṅkhakundendudhavalaṃ mṛṇālarajataprabham 
gokṣīrasadṛśaṃ tadvatsūryakoṭisamagrabham 
śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaṃ dhārayantaṃ caturbhujam  GarP 
kirīṭinaṃ kuṇḍalinaṃ vanamālāsamaṃnvitam 
sucakraṃ sukapolaṃ ca ṣītāmbaradharaṃ vibhum  GarP 
bhāvayitvā mahātmānaṃ sarvadevaiḥ samanvitam 
aṅgamantraistato nyāsaṃ mūlamantreṇa vai tathā  GarP 
tataśca darśayenmudrāṃ śaṅkhapadmādikāṃ śubhām 
dhyāyeddhyātvārcayedviṣṇuṃ mūlamantreṇa śaṅkara  GarP 
tataścāvāhayedrudra devatā āsanasya yāḥ 
oṃ hayagrīvāsanasya āgacchata ca devatāḥ  GarP 
āvāhya maṇḍale tāstu pūjayetsvastikādike 
dvāre dhāturvidhātuśca pūjā kāryā vṛṣadhvaja  GarP 
samastaparivārāya acyutāya nama iti 
asya madhyer'canaṃ kāryaṃ dvāre gaṅgāñca pūjayet  GarP 
yamunāṃ ca mahādevīṃ śaṅkhapadmanidhī tathā 
garuḍaṃ pūjayedagre madhye śaktiñca pūjayet  GarP 
ādhārākhyāṃ mahādeva tataḥ kūrmaṃ samarcayet 
anantaṃ pṛthivīṃ paścāddharmajñānenau
tato 'cayet  GarP 
vairāgyamatha caiśvaryamāgneyādiṣu pūjayet 
adharmājñānāvairāgyānaiśrargyādīṃstu pūrvataḥ  GarP 
sattvaṃ rajastamaścaiva madhyadeśe 'tha pūjayet 
kandaṃ nālaṃ ca padmaṃ ca madhye caiva prapūjayet  GarP 
arkasomāgnisaṃjñānāṃ maṇḍalānāṃ hi pūjanam 
madhyadeśe prakartavyamiti rudra prakīrtitam  GarP 
vimalotkarṣiṇī jñānā kriyāyoge vṛṣadhvaja 
prahvī satyā tatheśānānugrahau śaktayo hyamūḥ  GarP 
pūrvādiṣu ca patreṣu pūjyāśca vimalādayaḥ 
anugrahā karṇikāyāṃ pūjyā śreyo 'rthibhirnaraiḥ  GarP 
praṇavādyairnamo 'ntaiśca caturthyantaiśca nāmabhiḥ 
mantrairebhirmahādeva āsanaṃ paripūjayet  GarP 
snānagandhapradānena puṣpadhūpapradānataḥ 
dīpanaivedyadānena āsanasyārcanaṃ śubham  GarP 
kartavyaṃ vidhinānena iti te hara kīrtitam 
tataścāvāhayeddevaṃ hayagrīvaṃ sureśvaram  GarP 
vāmanāsāpuṭenaiva āgacchantaṃ vicintayet 
āgacchataḥ prayogeṇa mūlamantreṇa śaṅkara  GarP 
āvāhanaṃ prakartavyaṃ devadevasya śaṅkhinaḥ 
āvāhyamaṇḍale tasya nyāsaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ  GarP 
nyāsaṃ kṛtvā ca tatrasthaṃ cintayetparameśvaram 
hayagrīvaṃ mahādevaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam  GarP 
indrādilokapālaiśca saṃyuktaṃ viṣṇumavyayam 
dyātvā pradarśayenmudrāḥ śaṅkhacakrādikāḥ śubhāḥ  GarP 
pādyārghyācamanīyāni tato dadyācca viṣṇave 
snāpayecca tato devaṃ padmanābhamanāmayam  GarP 
devaṃ saṃsthāpya vidhivadvastraṃ dadyādvṛṣadhvaja 
tato hyācamanaṃ dadyādupavītaṃ tataḥ śubham  GarP 
tataśca maṇḍale rudra dhyāyeddevaṃ pareśvaram 
dhyātvā pādyādikaṃ bhūyo dadyāddevāya śaṅkara  GarP 
dadyādbhairavadevāya mūlamantreṇa śaṅkara 
oṃ kṣāṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ anena hṛdayaṃ yajet  GarP 
oṃ kṣīṃ śirase namaśca śirasaḥ pūjanaṃ bhavet 
oṃ kṣūṃ śikhāyai namaśca śikhāmetena pūjayet  GarP 
oṃ kṣaiṃ kavacāya namaḥ kavacaṃ paripūjayet 
oṃ kṣaiṃ netrāya namaśca netraṃ cānena pūjayet  GarP 
oṃ kṣaḥ astrāya nama iti astraṃ cānena pūjayet 
hṛdayaṃ ca śiraścaiva śikhāṃ ca kavacaṃ tathā  GarP 
pūrvādiṣu pradeśeṣu hyetāstu paripūjayet 
koṇeṣvastraṃ yajedrudra netraṃ madhyai prapūjayet  GarP 
pūjayetparamāṃ devīṃ lakṣmīṃ lakṣmīpradāṃ śubhām 
śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ tathā cakraṃ gadāṃ pūrvāditor'cayet  GarP 
khaḍgaṃ ca musalaṃ pāśamaṅkuśaṃ saśaraṃ dhanuḥ 
pūjayetpūrvato rudra ebhirmantraiḥ svanāmakaiḥ  GarP 
śrīvatsaṃ kaustubhaṃ mālāṃ tathā pītāmbaraṃ śubham 
pūjayetpūrvato rudra śaṅkhacakragadādharam  GarP 
brahmāṇaṃ nāradaṃ siddhaṃ guruṃ paraguruṃ tathā 
gurośca pāduke tadvatparamasya gurostathā  GarP 
indraṃ savāhanaṃ cātha parivārayutaṃ tathā 
agniṃ yamaṃ nirṛtiṃ ca varuṇaṃ vāyumeva ca  GarP 
somamīśānamevaṃ vai brahmāṇaṃ paripūjayet 
pūrvādikordhvaparyantaṃ pūjayedvṛṣabhadhvaja  GarP 
vajraṃ śaktiṃ tathā daṇḍaṃ khaṅgaṃ pāśaṃ dhvajaṃ gadām 
triśūlaṃ cakrapadme ca āyudhānyatha pūjayet  GarP 
viṣvaksenaṃ tato devamaiśānyāṃ diśi pūjayet 
ebhirmantrairnamo 'ntaiśca praṇavādyairvṛṣadhvaja  GarP 
pūjā kāryā mahādeva hyanantasya vṛṣadhvaja 
devasya mūlamantreṇa pūjā kāryā vṛṣadhvaja  GarP 
gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ naivedyameva ca 
pradakṣiṇaṃ namaskāraṃ japyaṃ tasmai samarpayet  GarP 
stuvīta cānyā stutyā praṇavādyairvṛṣadhvaja 
oṃ namo hayaśirase vidyādhyakṣāya vai namaḥ  GarP 
namo vidyāsvarūpāya vidyādātre namonamaḥ 
namaḥ śāntāya devāya triguṇāyātmane namaḥ  GarP 
surāsuranihantre ca sarvaduṣṭavināśine 
sarvalokādhipataye brahmarūpāya vai namaḥ  GarP 
namaśceśvaravandyāya śaṅkacakradhāraya ca 
nama ādyāya dāntāya sarvasattvahitāya ca  GarP 
triguṇāyāguṇāyaiva brahmaviṣṇusvarūpiṇe 
kartre hartre sureśāya sarvagāya namonamaḥ  GarP 
ityevaṃ saṃstavaṃ kṛtvā devadevaṃ vicintayet 
hṛtpadme vimale rudra śaṅkhacakragadādharam  GarP 
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ sarvāvayavasundaram 
hayagrīvomahīśeśaṃ paramātmānamavyayam  GarP 
iti te kathitā pūjā hayagrīvasya śaṅkara 
yaḥ paṭhetparayā bhaktyā sa gacchetparamaṃ padam  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe hayagrīvapūjāvidhirnāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
hariruvāca 
nyāsādikaṃ pravakṣyāmi gāyattryāḥ śṛṇu śaṅkara 
viśvāmitraṛṣiścaiva savitā cātha devatā  GarP 
brahmaśīrṣā rudraśikhā viṣṇorhṛdayasaṃśritā 
viniyogaikanayanā kātyāyanasagotrajā  GarP 
trailokyacaraṇā jñeyā pṛthivīkukṣisaṃsthitā 
evaṃ jñātvā tu gāyattrīṃ japeddvādaśalakṣakam  GarP 
tripadāṣṭākṣarā jñeyā catuṣpādā ṣaḍakṣarā 
jepa ca tripadā groktā arcane ca catuṣpadā  GarP 
nyāse jape tathā dhyāne agnikārye tathārcane 
gāyattrīṃ vinyasennityaṃ sarvapāpagraṇāśinīm  GarP 
pādāṃsuṣṭhe gulphamadhye jaṅghayorviddhi jānunoḥ 
ūrvorguhye ca vṛṣaṇe nāḍyāṃ nābhau tanūdare  GarP 
stanayorhṛdi kaṇṭhauṣṭhamukhe tāluni cāṃsayoḥ 
netre bhuvārlalāṭe ca pūrvasyāṃ dakṣiṇottare  GarP 
paścame mūrdhni cākāraṃ nyasedvarṇānvadāmyaham 
indranīlaṃ ca vahniṃ ca pītaṃ śyāmaṃ ca kāpilam  GarP 
śvetaṃ vidyutprabhaṃ tāraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ raktaṃ krameṇa tat 
śyāmaṃ śuklaṃ tathā pītaṃ śvetaṃ vai padmarāgavat  GarP 
śaṅkhavarṇaṃ pāṇḍuraṃ ca raktaṃ cāsavasannibham 
arkavarṇasamaṃ saumyaṃ śaṅkhābhaṃ śvetameva ca  GarP 
yadyatspṛśati hastena yacca paśyati cakṣuṣā 
pūtaṃ bhavati tatsarvaṃ gāyattryā na paraṃ viduḥ  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe gāyattrīnyāsanirūpaṇaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
hariruvāca 
sandhyāvidhiṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu rudrāghanāśanam 
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā sandhyāsnānamupakramet  GarP 
sapraṇavāṃ savyāhṛtiṃ gāyattrīṃ śirasā saha 
triḥ paṭhedāyatapraṇaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa ucyate  GarP 
manovākrāyajaṃ doṣaṃ prāṇāyāmairdaheddvijaḥ 
tasmātsarveṣu kāleṣu prāṇāyāmaparo bhavet  GarP 
sāyamagniśca metyuktā prātaḥ sūryetyapaḥ pibet 
āpaḥ punantu madhyāhne upaspṛśya yathāvidhi  GarP 
āpohiṣṭhetyṛcā kuryānmārjanaṃ tu kuśodakaiḥ 
praṇavena tu saṃyuktaṃ kṣipedvāri padepade  GarP 
rajastamaḥ svamohotthāñjāgratsvapnasuṣuptijān 
vāṅmanaḥ karmajāndoṣānnavaitānnavabhirdahet  GarP 
samuddhṛtyodakaṃ pāṇau japtvā ca drupadāṃ kṣipet 
tripaḍaṣṭau dvādaśadhā vartayedaghamarpaṇam  GarP 
udutyañcitramityābhyāmupatiṣṭheddivākaram 
divā rātrau ca yatpāpaṃ sarvaṃ naśyati tatkṣaṇāt  GarP 
pūrvasaṃdhyāṃ japaṃstiṣṭhetpaścimāmupaviśya ca 
mahāvyāhṛtisaṃyuktāṃ gāyattrīṃ praṇavānvitām  GarP 
daśabhirjanmajanitaṃ śatena tu purā kṛtam 
triyugaṃ tu sahasreṇa gāyattrī hanti duṣkṛtam  GarP 
raktā bhavati gāyattrī sāvitrī śuklavarṇikā 
kṛṣṇā sarasvatī jñeyā saṃdhyātrayamudāhṛtam  GarP 
oṃ bhūrvinyasya hṛdaye oṃ bhuvaḥ śirasi nyaset 
oṃ svariti śikhāyāṃ ca gāyattryāḥ prathamaṃ padam  GarP 
vinyasetkavace vidvāndvitīyaṃ netrayornyaset 
tṛtīyenāṅgavinyāsaṃ caturthaṃ sarvato nyaset  GarP 
saṃdhyākāle tu vinyasya japedvai vedamātaram 
śivastasyāstu sarvāhne prāṇāyāmaparaṃ nyaset  GarP 
tripadā yā tu gāyattrī brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarī 
viniyogamṛṣicchando jñātvā tu japamārabhet  GarP 
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmalokamavāpnuyāt 
parorajasi sāvadoṃ turīyapadamīritam  GarP 
taṃ hanti sūryaḥ sandhyāyāṃ nopāstiṃ kurute tu yaḥ 
turīyasya padasyāpi ṛṣirnirmala eva ca  GarP 
chandastu devī gāyattrī paramātmā ca devatā  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe saṃdhyāvidhirnāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

hariruvāca 
gāyattrī paramā devī bhuktimuktipradā ca tām 
yo japettasya pāpānivinaśyanti mahāntyapi  GarP 
gāyattrīkalpamākhyāsye bhuktimuktipradaṃ ca tat 
aṣṭottaraṃ sahasraṃ vā athavāṣṭaśataṃ japet  GarP 
trisandhyaṃ brahmalokīsyācchataṃ japtvā jalaṃ pibet 
saṃdhyāyāṃ sarvapāpaghnīṃ devīmāvāhya pūjayet  GarP 
bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ svamantreṇa yutāṃ dvādaśanāmabhiḥ 
gāyatryai namaḥ 
sāvitryai sarasvatyai namonamaḥ  GarP 
vedamātre ca sāṃkṛtyai brahmāṇī kauśikī kramāt 
sādhvyai sarvārthasādhinyai sahasrākṣyai ca bhūrbhuvaḥ  GarP 
svarevaṃ juhuyā dagnau samidājyaṃ haviṣyakam 
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ vāpyathavāṣṭaśanta ghṛtam  GarP 
dharmakāmādisiddhyarthaṃ juhuyātsarvakarmasu 
pratimāṃ candanasvarṇanirmitāṃ pratipūjya ca  GarP 
yathā lakṣaṃ tu japtavyaṃ payomūlaphalārśanaiḥ 
ayutadvayahomena sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt  GarP 
uttare śikhare jātā bhūmyāṃ parvata vāsinī 
brahmaṇā samanujñātā gaccha devi yathāsukham  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe gāyattrīkalpanirūpaṇaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

hariruvāca 
navamyādau yajeddurgāṃ hrīṃ durge rakṣiṇīti ca 
mātarmātarvare durge sarvakāmārthasādhani  GarP 
anena balidānena sarvakāmānprayaccha me 
gaurī kālī umā durgā bhadrā kāntiḥ sarasvatī  GarP 
maṅgalā vijayā lakṣmīḥ śivā nārāyaṇī kramāt 
mārge tṛtīyāmārabhya pūjayenna viyogabhāk  GarP 
aṣṭādaśabhujāṃ kheṭakaṃ ghaṇṭāṃ darpaṇaṃ tarjanīm 
dhanurdhvajaṃ ḍamarukaṃ paraśuṃ pāśameva ca  GarP 
śaktimudraraśūlāni kapālaśarakāṅkuśān 
vajra cakraṃ śalākāṃ ca aṣṭādaśabhujāṃ smaret  GarP 
mantraḥ śrībhagavatyāśca pravakṣyāmi japādikam  GarP 
oṃ namo bhagavati cāmuṇḍe śmaśānavāsini kapālahaste mahāpretasamārūḍhe mahāvimānamālākule
kālarātri bahugaṇaparivṛte mahāmukhe bahubhuje sughaṇṭāḍamarukiṅkiṇīke aṭṭāṭṭahāse
kilikili huṃ sarvanādaśabdabahule gajacarmaprāvṛtaśarīre rudhiramāṃsadigdhe lolagrajihve
mahārākṣasi raudradaṃṣṭrākarāle bhīmāṭṭāṭṭahāse sphuritavidyutsamaprabhe calacala
karālanetre hilihili lalajjihve hraiṃ hrīṃ bhṛkuṭimukhi oṃ kārabhadrāsane kapālamālāveṣṭite
jaṭāmukuṭaśaśāṅkadhāriṇi aṭṭāṭṭahāse kilikili huṃhuṃ daṃṣṭrāghorāndhakāriṇi sarvavighnavināśini
idaṃ karma sādhaya sādhaya śīghraṃ kurukuru kahakaha aṅkuśe samanupraveśaya vargaṃvargaṃ vaṅgavaṅga
kampayakampaya calacala cālayacālaya rudhiramāṃsamadyapriye hanahana kuṭṭakuṭṭa chindachinda
mārayamāraya anubūma anubūma vajraśarīraṃ sādhayasādhaya trailokyagatamapi duṣṭamaduṣṭaṃ
vā gṛhītamagṛhītam āveśaya āveśaya krāmayakramaya nṛtyanṛtya bandhabandha valgavalga
koṭarākṣi urdhvakeśi ulūkavadane karakiṅkiṇi karaṅkamālādhāriṇi dahadaha pacapaca
gṛhṇagahṇa maṇḍalamadhye praveśayapraveśaya kiṃ vilambasi brahmasatyena viṣṇusatyena
ṛṣisatyena rudrasatyena āveśaya āveśaya kilikili khilikhili milimili cilicili vikṛtarūpadhāriṇi
kṛṣṇabhujaṅga veṣṭitaśarīra sarvagrahāveśini pralambhoṣṭhi bhrūmagnanāsike vikaṭamukhi
kapilajaṭe brāhmi bhañjabhañja jvalajvala kālamukhi khalakhala kharakharaḥ pātayapā
taya raktākṣi dhūrṇāpayadhūrṇāpaya bhūmiṃ pātayapātaya śiro gṛhṇagṛhṇa cakṣurmolayamīlaya
bhañjabhañja pādau gṛhṇagṛhṇa mudrāṃ sphoṭayasphoṭaya huṃ hūṃ phaṭ vidāraya vidāraya
triśūlena bhedayabhedaya vajreṇa hanahana daṇḍena tāḍayatāḍaya cekraṇa chedayachedaya
śaktinā bhedayabhedaya
 daṃṣṭrayā daṃśayadaṃśaya kīlakena kīlaya kīlaya kartārikayā pāṭayapāṭaya aṅkuśena gṛhṇagṛhṇa brahmāṇi ehi ehi māheśvari ehi ehi kaumāri ehi  
ehi vārāhi ehi ehi 
aindri ehi ehi cāmuṇḍe ehi ehi vaiṣṇāvi ehi ehi himavantacāriṇi ehi ehi kailāsavārīṇi
ehi ehi paramantraṃ chindhichindhi kilikili bimbe aghore ghorarūpiṇi cāmuṇḍe rurukrodhāndhaviniḥ
sṛte asurakṣayaṅkari ākāśagāmini pāśena bandhabandha samaye tiṣṭhatiṣṭha maṇḍalaṃ
praveśayapraveśaya pātayapātaya gṛhṇagṛhṇa mukhaṃ bandhabandha cakṣurbandhayabandhaya
hṛdayaṃ bandhabandha hastapādau ca bandhabandha duṣṭagrahān sarvān bandhabandha diśāṃ
bandhabandha vidiśāṃ bandhabandha ūrdhvaṃ bandhabandha adhastād bandhabandha bhasmanā
pānīyena mṛtikayā sarṣapairvā āveśaya āveśaya pātayapātaya cāmuṇḍe kilikili vicchehrīṃhuṃ
phaṭ svāh  GarP 
aṣṭottarapadānāṃ hi mālā mantramayī japaḥ 
ekaikrapadamaṣṭasahasradhā trimadhurāktatilāṣṭasahasrahāmeḥ  GarP 
mahāmāṃsenatrimadhurāktena aṣṭottarasahsatraṃ ca ekaikaṃ ca padaṃ yajet 
tilāṃstrimadhurāktāṃśca sahasraṃ cāṣṭa homayet  GarP 
mahāmāṃsaṃ trimadhurādatha vā sarvakarmakṛt 
vārisarṣapabhasmādikṣepādyuddhādike jayaḥ  GarP 
aṣṭāviṃśabhujā dhyeyā aṣṭādaśabhujāthavā 
dvādaśāṣṭabhujā vāpi dhyeyā vāpi caturbhujā  GarP 
asikheṭānvitau hastau gadādaṇḍayutau parau 
śaracāpayutau cānyau khaḍgamudrarasaṃyutau  GarP 
khaṅkhaghaṇṭānvitau cānyau dhvajadaṇḍayutau parau 
anyau paraśucakrāḍhyau ḍamarudarpaṇānvitau  GarP 
śaktihastāśritau cānyau raṭoṇī musalānvitau 
pāśatomarasaṃyuktau ḍhakrāpaṇavasaṃyutau  GarP 
tarjayantī pareṇaiva anyaṃ kalakaladhvanim 
abhayasvastikādyau ca mahiṣaghnī ca siṃhagā  GarP 
jaya tvaṃ kila bhūteśe sarvabhūtasamāvṛte 
rakṣa māṃ nijabhūtebhyo valiṃ gṛhṇa namo 'stu te  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe durgājapapūjābalimantranirūpaṇaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
rudra uvāca 
punardevārcanaṃ brūhi saṃkṣepeṇa janārdana 
sūryasya viṣṇurūpasya bhuktimuktipradāyakam  GarP 
vāsudeva uvāca 
śṛṇu sūryasya rudra tvaṃ punarvakṣyāmi pūjanam 
oṃ uccaiḥ śravase namaḥ oṃ aruṇāya namaḥ 
oṃ daṇḍine namaḥ 
oṃ piṅgalāya namaḥ 
ete dvāre prapūjyā vai epirmantrairvṛṣadhvaja  GarP 
oṃ aṃ prabhūtāya namaḥ 
imaṃ tu pūjayenmadhye prabhūtāmalasaṃjñakam 
oṃ aṃ vimalāya namaḥ 
oṃ aṃ sārāya namaḥ 
oṃ aṃādhārāya namaḥ 
oṃ aṃ paramamukhāya namaḥ 
ityāgneyādikoṇeṣu pūjyā vai vimalādayaḥ  GarP 
oṃ padmāya namaḥ 
oṃ karṇikāyai namaḥ

oṃ arkāsanāya namaḥ

oṃ haṃ saṃ khaṃ khakholkāya krāṃ krīṃ saḥ svāhā sūryamūrtaye namaḥ 
anenāvāhanaṃ kuryātsthāpanaṃ sannidhāpanam 
sanniropanamantreṇa sakalīkaraṇaṃ tathā  GarP

tejorūpaṃ raktavarṇaṃ sitapadmopari sthitam 
ekacakrarathārūḍhaṃ dvibāhuṃ dhṛtapaṅkajam  GarP 
evaṃ dhyāyetsadā sūryaṃ mūlamantraṃ śṛṇuṣva ca 
oṃ hrāṃ hrīṃ saḥ sūryāya namaḥ  GarP 
vāratrayaṃ padmamudrāṃ bimbamudrāṃ ca darśayet 
oṃ āṃ hṛdayāya namaḥ 
oṃ arkāya śirase svāhā 
oṃ aḥ bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ jvālini śikhāyai vaṣaṭ 
oṃ huṃ kavacāya huṃ 
oṃ bhāṃ netrābhyāṃ vauṣaṭ 
oṃ vaḥ astrāya phaḍiti  GarP 
āgneyyāmathavaiśānyāṃ nairṛtyāmarcayeddhara 
tdṛyadayādi hi vāyavyāṃ netraṃ cāntaḥ prapūjayet  GarP 
disvastraṃ pūjayedrudra somaṃ tu śvetavarṇakam 
dale pūrver'cayedrudra budhaṃ cāmīkaraprabham  GarP 
dakṣiṇe pūjayedrudra pativarṇaṃ guruṃ yajet 
paścime caiva bhūteśaṃ uttare bhārgavaṃ sitam  GarP 
raktamaṅgārakaṃ caiva āgneye pūjayeddhara 
śanaiścaraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ nairṛtyāṃ diśi pūjayet  GarP 
rāhuṃ vāyavyadeśe tu nandyāvartanibhiṃ hara 
aiśānyāṃ dhūmravarṇaṃ tu ketuṃ saṃ paripūjayet  GarP 
ebhirmantrairmahādeva tacchṛṇuṣva ca śaṅkara  GarP 
oṃ soṃ somāya namaḥ 
oṃ buṃ budhāya namaḥ 
oṃ bṛṃ bṛhaspataye namaḥ 
oṃ bhaṃ bhārgavāya namaḥ 
oṃ aṃ aṅgārakāya namaḥ

oṃ raṃ rāhave namaḥ 
oṃ kaṃ ketave nama iti  GarP 
pādyādīnmūlamantreṇa dattvā sūryāya śaṅkara 
naivedyānte dhenumudrāṃ darśayetsādhakottamaḥ  GarP 
japtvā cāṣṭasahasraṃ tu tacca tasmai samarpayet 
aiśānyāṃ diśi bhūteśa tejaścaṇḍaṃ tu pūjayet  GarP 
oṃ tejaścaṃṇḍāya huṃ phaṭ svadhā svāhā pauṣaṭ

kṛtvā śirasi tatpātraṃ jānubhyāmavaniṃ gataḥ 
darghyaṃ tu sūryāya tdṛnmantreṇa vṛṣadhvaja  GarP

oṃ gaṃ gaṇapataye namaḥ

sūryasya kathitā pūjā kṛtvaitāṃ viṣṇulokabhāk  GarP

oṃ viśvāvasurnāma gandharvaḥ kanyānāmadhipatirlabhāmi te kanyāṃ samutpādya tasmai viśvavāsave svāhā

hariruvāca 
pavitrāropaṇaṃ vakṣye bhuktimuktipradaṃ hareḥ 
purā devāsure yuddhe brahmādyāḥ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ  GarP 
viṣṇuśca teṣāṃ devānāṃ dhvajaṃ graiveyakaṃ dadau 
etau dṛṣṭvā vinaṅkṣyanti dānavānabravīddhariḥ  GarP 
viṣṇūkte hyabravīnnāgo vāsukeranujastadā 
vṛṇīta ca vapitrākhyaṃ varaṃ cedaṃ vṛṣadhvaja  GarP 
graiveyaṃ haridattaṃ tu mannāmnā khyātimeṣyati 
ityukte tena te devāstannāmnā tadvaraṃ viduḥ  GarP 
prāvṛṭkāle tu ye martyā nārciṣyanti pavitrakaiḥ 
teṣāṃ sāṃvatsarī pūjā viphalā ca bhaviṣyati  GarP 
tasmātsarveṣu deveṣu pavitrāropaṇaṃ kramāt 
pratipatpaurṇamāsyāntā yasya yā tithirucyate  GarP 
dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇave kāryaṃ śukle kṛṣṇe 'tha vā hara 
vyatīpāte 'yane caiva candarasūryagrahe śiva  GarP 
viṣṇave vṛddhikārye ca gurorāgamane tathā 
nityaṃ pavitramuddiṣṭaṃ prāvṛṭkāle tvavaśyakam  GarP 
kauśeyaṃ paṭṭasūtraṃ vā kārpāsaṃ kṣaumameva vā 
kuśasūtra dvijānāṃ syādrājñā kauśeyapaṭṭakam  GarP 
vaiśyānāṃ cīraṇaṃ kṣaumaṃ śūdrāṇāṃ śaṇavalkajam 
kārpāsaṃ padmajaṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śastamīśvara  GarP 
brāhmaṇyā kartitaṃ sūtraṃ triguṇaṃ triguṇīkṛtam 
oṃ kāro 'tha śivaḥ somo hyagnirbrahyā phaṇī raviḥ  GarP 
vighneśo viṣṇurityete sthitāstantuṣu devatāḥ 
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca trisūtre devatāḥ smṛtāḥ  GarP 
sauvarṇe rājate tāmre vaiṇave mṛnmaye nyaset 
aṅguṣṭhena catuḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ śreṣṭhaṃ madhyaṃ tadardhataḥ  GarP 
tadardhā tu kaniṣṭhā syātsūtramaṣṭottaraṃ śatam 
uttamaṃ madhyamaṃ caiva kanyasaṃ pūrvavatkramāt  GarP 
uttamoṃ'guṣṭhamānena madhyamo madhyamena tu 
kanyase ca kaniṣṭhena aṅgulyā granthayaḥ smṛtāḥ  GarP 
vimāne sthaṇḍile caiva etatsāmānyalakṣaṇam 
śivoddhṛtaṃ pavitraṃ tu pratimāyāṃ ca kārayet  GarP 
hṛnnābhirūru
rumāne ca jānubhyāmavalambinī 
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa catvāro granthayaḥ smṛtāḥ  GarP 
ṣaṭtriṃḍviṃ
śacca caturviśaddvādaśa granthayo 'thavā 
uttamādiṣu vijñeyāḥ parvabhirvā pavitrakam  GarP 
carcitaṃ kuṅkumenaiva haridrācandanena vā 
sopavāsaḥ pavitrantu pātrasthamadhivāsayet  GarP 
aśvatthapatrapuṭake aṣṭadikṣu niveśitam 
daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ kuśāgraṃ ca pūrve saṅkarṣaṇena tu  GarP 
rocanākuṅkumenava pradyumnena tu dakṣiṇe 
yuddhārtho phalasiddhyarthamaniruddhena paścime  GarP 
candanaṃ nīlayuktaṃ ca tilabhasmākṣataṃ tathā 
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣur śyādīnāṃ tu kramānnyaset  GarP 
pavitraṃ vāsudevena abhimantrya sakṛtsakṛt 
dṛṣṭvā punaḥ prapūjyātha vastreṇācchādya yatnataḥ  GarP 
devasya purataḥ sthāpyaṃ pratimāmaṇḍalasya vā 
paścime dakṣiṇe caiva uttare pūrvavatkramāt  GarP 
brāhmādīṃścāpi saṃsthāpya kalaśaṃ cāpi pūjayet 
astreṇa maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā naivedyañca samarpayet  GarP 
adhivāsya pavitraṃ tu trisūtreṇa navena vā ca 
vedikāṃ veṣṭayitvā tu ātmānaṃma kalaśaṃ ghṛtam  GarP 
agnikuṇḍaṃ vimānaṃ ca maṇḍapaṃ gṛhameva ca 
sūtramekaṃ tu saṃgṛhya dadyāddevasya mṛrdhāni  GarP 
dattvā paṭhedimaṃ mantraṃ pūjayitvā maheśvaram 
āvāhito 'si deveśa pūjārthaṃ parameśvara  GarP 
tatprabhāter'cayiṣyāmi sāmagyāḥ sannidhau bhava 
ekarātraṃ trirātraṃ vā adhivāsya pavitrakam  GarP 
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prātaḥ saṃpūjya keśavam 
āropayetkrameṇaiva jyeṣṭhamadhyakanīyasam  GarP 
dhūpayitvā pavitraṃ tu mantreṇaivābhimantrayet 
prajaptagranthikaṃ caiva pūjayetkusumādibhiḥ  GarP 
gāyattryā cārcitaṃ tena devaṃ saṃpūjya dāpayet 
samaṃ putrakalatrādyaiḥ sūtrapucchaṃ tu dhārayet  GarP 
viśuddhagranthikaṃ ramyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam 
sarvapāpakṣayaṃ deva tavāgre dhārayāmyaham  GarP 
evaṃ dhūpādinābhyarcya madhyamādīntsamarpayet 
pavitraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaḥ sarvapātakanāśanam  GarP 
dharmakāmārthasiddhyarthaṃ svakaṇṭhe dhārayāmyaham 
vanamālāṃ samabhyarcya svena mantreṇa dāpayet  GarP 
naivedyaṃ vividhaṃ dattvā kusumāderbaliṃ haret 
agniṃ saṃtarpya tatrāpi dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ  GarP 
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva dadyādekapavitrakam 
ādau dattvārghyamāditye tatra caikaṃ pavitrakam  GarP 
viṣvaksenaṃ tataḥ prārcya surumarghyādibhirhara 
devasyāgre paṭhenmantraṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ sthitaḥ  GarP 
jñānato 'jñānato vāpi pūjanādi kṛtaṃ mayā 
tatsarvaṃ pūrṇamevāstu tvatprasādātsureśvara  GarP 
maṇividrumamālabhirmandārakusumādibhiḥ 
iyaṃ sāṃvatsarī pūjā tavāstu garuḍadhvaja  GarP 
vanamālā yathā deva kaustubhaṃ satataṃ hṛdi 
tadvatpavitraṃ tantūnāṃ mālāṃ tvaṃ hṛdaye dhara  GarP 
evaṃ prārthya dvijān bhojya dattvā tebhyaśca dakṣiṇām 
visarjayettu tenaiva sāyāhne tvapare 'hani  GarP 
sāṃvatsarīmimāṃ pūjāṃ sampādya vidhivanmayā 
vrajeḥ pavitrakedānīṃ viṣṇulekaṃ visarjitaḥ  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe viṣṇupavitrāropaṇaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
hariruvāca 
pūjayitvā pavitrādyairbrahma dhyātvā harirbhavet 
brahmadhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi māyāyantrapramardakam  GarP 
yacchedvāṅmanasaṃ prājñastaṃ yajejjñānamātmani 
jñānaṃ mahati saṃyacchedya icchejjñānamātmāni  GarP 
dehendriyamanobuddhiprāṇāhaṅkarāvarjitam 
varjitaṃ bhūtatanmātrairguṇajanmāśanādibhiḥ  GarP 
svaprakāśaṃ nirākāraṃ sadānaṃ damanādi yat 
nityaṃ śuddhaṃ buddhamṛddhaṃ satyamānandamadvayam  GarP 
turīyamakṣaraṃ brahma ahamasmi paraṃ padam 
ahaṃ brahmetyavasthānaṃ samādhirapi riti gīyate  GarP 
ātmānaṃ rathinaṃ viddhi śarīraṃ rathameva tu 
buddhiṃ ca sārathiṃ viddhi manaḥ pragrahameva ca 
indriyāṇi hayānāhurviṣayāsteṣu gocarāḥ  GarP 
ātmendriyamanoyukto bhoktetyārmanīṣiṇaḥ 
yastu vijñāna bāhmena yuktena manasā sadā  GarP 
sa tu tatpadamāpnoti sa hi bhūyo na jāyate 
vijñānasārathiryastu manaḥ pragrahavānnaraḥ  GarP 
svardhunyāḥ pāramāpnoti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam 
ahiṃsādiryamaḥ proktaḥ śaucādirniyamaḥ smṛtaḥ  GarP 
āsanaṃ padmakādyuktaṃ prāṇāyāmo marujjayaḥ 
pratyāhā ro jayaḥ prokto dhyānamīśvaracintanam  GarP 
manodhṛtirdhāraṇā sthātsamādhirbrahmaṇi sthitiḥ 
pūrvaṃ cetaḥ sthiraṃ na syāttatomūrtiṃ vicintayet  GarP 
hṛtpadmakarṇikāmadhye śaṅkhacakragadābjavān 
śrīvatsakaustubhayuto vanamālāśriyā yutaḥ  GarP 
nityaḥ śuddho bhūtiyuktaḥ satyānandāhvayaḥ paraḥ 
ātmāhaṃ paramaṃ brahma paramaṃ jyotireva tu  GarP 
caturviśatimūrtiḥ sa śālagrāmaśilāsthitaḥ 
dvārakādiśilāsaṃstho dhyeyaḥ pūjyo 'pyahaṃ ca saḥ  GarP 
manaso 'bhīpsitaṃ prāpya devo vaimāniko bhavet 
niṣkāmo muktimāpnoti mūrtiṃ dhyāyayaṃstuvañjapan  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe brahmamūrtidhyānanirūpaṇaṃ nāma catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
hariruvāca 
prasaṃgātkathayiṣyāmi śālagrāmasya lakṣaṇam 
śālagrāmaśilāsparśātkoṭijanmāghanāśanam  GarP 
śakhacakragadāpadmī hastaḥ
keśavākhyo
gadādharaḥ 
sabjakaumādakīcakraśaṅkhī nārāyaṇo vibhuḥ  GarP 
sacakraśaṅkhābjagado mādhavaḥ
śrīgadādharaḥ 
gadabjaśaṅkhacakrī vā govindo
'rcyo gadādharaḥ  GarP 
padmaśaṅkhārigādine viṣṇurūpāya te namaḥ 
saśaṅkhābjagadācakra madhusūdanamūrtaye  GarP 
namo gadāriśaṅkhābjayuktatraivikramāya ca 
sārikaumodakīpadmaśaṅkhavāmanamūrtaye  GarP 
cakrābjaśaṅkhagādine namaḥ śrīdharamūrtaye 
hṛṣīkeśāyā
'bjagadāśaṅkhine cakriṇe namaḥ  GarP 
sābjacakragadāśaṅkhapadmanābhasvarūpiṇe 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmin dāmodara
manonamaḥ  GarP 
sāriśaṅkhagadābjāya vāsudevāya vai namaḥ 
śaṅkhābjacakragādine namaḥ saṅkarṣaṇāya ca  GarP 
suśaṅkhasugadābjāridhṛte pradyumnamūrtaye 
namo'niruddhāya
gadāśaṅkhābjārīvidhāriṇe  GarP 
sābjaśaṅkhagadācakrapuruṣottamamūrtaye 
namo'dhokṣajarūpāya
gadāśaṅkhāripadmine  GarP 
nṛsiṃhamūrtaye
padmagadāśaṅkhāridhāriṇe 
padmāriśaṅkhagadine namo 'stvacyutamūrtaye  GarP 
saśaṅkacakrābjagadaṃ janārdana mihānaye 
upendraḥ sagadaḥ sāriḥ padmaśaṅkhinnamonamaḥ  GarP 
sucakrābjagadāśaṅkhayuktāya harimūrtaye 
sagadābjāriśaṅkhāya namaḥ śrīkṛṣṇamūrtaye  GarP 
śālagrāmaśilādvāragatalagnadvicakradhṛk 
śuklābhovāsudevākhyaḥ
so 'vyādvaḥ śrīgadādharaḥ  GarP 
lagnadvicakro raktābhaḥ pūrvabhāgastupuṣkalaḥ 
saṃkarṣaṇo 'thapradyumnaḥ
sūkṣmacakrastu pītakaḥ  GarP 
sa dīrghaḥ saśiraśchidro yo'niruddhastu vartulaḥ 
nīlo dvāri trirekhaśca atha nārāyaṇo'sitaḥ  GarP 
madhye gādakṛtī rekhā nābhicakro kra
mahonnataḥ 
pṛthuvakṣā nṛsiṃho
vaḥ kapilo 'vyāttribindukaḥ  GarP 
athavā pañcabindustatpūjanaṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ 
varāhaḥ śaktiliṅgo 'vyādviṣamadvayacakrakaḥ  GarP 
nīlastrirekhaḥ sthūlo 'tha kūrmamūrtiḥ sa bindumān 
kṛṣṇaḥ sa vartulāvartaḥ pātu vo natapṛṣṭhakaḥ  GarP 
śrīdharaḥ pañcarekho 'vyā dvanamālī
gādāṅkitaḥ 
vāmano vartulo hrasvo vā rā
macakraḥ sureśvaraḥ  GarP 
nānāvarṇo 'nekamūrtirnāgabhogī tvanantakaḥ 
sthūlo dāmodaro
nīlo madhyevakraḥ sunīlakaḥ  GarP 
saṃkīrṇadvārakaḥ so 'vyādatha brahmā sulohitaḥ 
sadīrgharekhaḥ suṣira ekacakrāmbujaḥ pṛthuḥ  GarP 
pṛthucchidraḥ sthūlacakraḥkṛṣṇo
viṣṇuśca bilvavat 
hayagrīvo 'ṅkuśākāraḥ pañcarekhaḥ sakaustubhaḥ  GarP 
vaikuṇṭho maṇiratnābha ekacakrāmbujo 'sitaḥ 
matsyo dīrgho 'mbujākāro dvārarekhaśca pātu vaḥ  GarP 
rāmacakro dakṣarekhaḥ śyāmovo 'vyā ttrivikramaḥ 
śālagrāme dvārakāyāṃ sthitāya gadina namaḥ  GarP 
ekadvāraścatuścakro vanamālāvibhūṣitaḥ 
svarṇarekhāsamāyukto goṣpadena virājitaḥ  GarP 
kadambakusumākāro lakṣmīnārāyaṇo'vatu 
ekena lakṣito yovyādradādhārī sudarśanaḥ  GarP 
lakṣmīnārāyaṇo
dvābhyāntribhirmūrtistrivikramaḥ 
caturbhiśca caturvyūho
vāsudevaśca
pañcabhiḥ  GarP 
pradyumnaḥ
ṣaḍūbhireva syāt saṃkarṣaṇa itastataḥ 
puruṣottamo
'ṣṭabhiḥ syānnavavyūho
navāṅkitaḥ  GarP 
daśāvatāro
daśabhiraniruddho 'vatādatha 
dvādaśātmā
dvādaśabirata ūrdhvamanantakaḥ  GarP 
viṣṇormūrtimayaṃ stotraṃ yaḥ paṭhetsa divaṃ vrajet 
brahmā caturmukho daṇḍī kamaṇḍaluyugānvitaḥ  GarP 
maheśvaraḥ
prañcavakro daśabāhurvṛṣadhvajaḥ 
yathāyudhastathā gaurī caṇḍikā ca sarasvatī  GarP 
mahālakṣmīrmātaraśca padmahasto divākaraḥ 
gajāsyaśca gaṇaḥ skandaḥ ṣaṇmukhonekadhā guṇāḥ  GarP 
ete 'rcitāḥ sthāpitāśca prāsāde vāstupūjite 
dharmārthakāmamokṣādyāḥ prāpyante puruṣeṇa ca  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe śālagrāmamūrtilakṣaṇaṃ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
hariruvāca 
vāstuṃ saṃkṣepato vakṣye gṛhādau vighnanāśanam 
īsānakoṇādārabhya hyekāśītipade yajet  GarP 
īśāne ca śiraḥ pādau nairṛte 'gnyanile karau 
āvāsavāsaveśmādau pure grāme vaṇikpathe  GarP 
prāsādārāmadurgeṣu devālayamaṭheṣu ca 
dvāviṃśati surānbāhye tadantaśca trayodaśa  GarP 
īśaścaivātha parjanyo jayantaḥ kuliśāyudhaḥ 
sūryaḥ satyo bhṛguścaiva ākāśo vāyureva ca  GarP 
pūṣā ca vitathaścaiva grahakṣetrayamāvubhau 
gandharvo bhṛgurājastu mṛgaḥ pitṛgaṇastathā  GarP 
dauvāriko 'tha sugrīvaḥ puṣpadanto gaṇādhipaḥ 
asuraḥ śeṣapāpau dau ca rogo
ḍahimukha khya eva ca  GarP 
bhallāṭaḥ somasarpau ca aditiścaditistathā 
bahirdvātriṃśadete tu tadantaścaturaḥ śṛṇu  GarP 
īśānādicatuṣkoṇasaṃsthitānpūjayeddhudhaḥ 
āpaścaivātha sāvitrī jayo rudrastathaiva ca  GarP 
madhye navapade brahmā tasyāṣṭhau ca samīpagān 
devānekottarānetānpūrvādau nāmataḥ śṛṇu  GarP 
aryamā savitā caiva vivasvānvibudhādhipaḥ 
mitro 'tha rājayakṣmā ca tathā pṛthvīdharaḥ kramāt  GarP 
aṣṭamaścāpavatsaśca parito brahmaṇaḥ smṛtāḥ 
īśānakoṇādārabhya durge car jñeyo
vaṃśa ucyate  GarP 
āgneyakoṇādārabhya vaṃśo bhavati durdharaḥ 
aditiṃ himavantaṃ ca jayantaṃ ca idaṃ trayam  GarP 
nāyikā kālikā nāma śakrādrandharvagāḥ punaḥ 
vāstudevānpūjayitvā gṛhaprāsādakṛdbhavet  GarP 
surejyaḥ purataḥ kāryo yasyāgneyyāṃ mahānasam 
kapinirgamane ṇī
yena pūrvataḥ satramaṇḍapam  GarP 
gandhapuṣpagṛhaṃ kāryamaiśānyāṃ paṭṭasaṃyutam 
bhāṇḍāgāraṃ ca kauberyāṃ goṣṭhāgāraṃ ca vāyave  GarP 
udagāśrayaṃ ca vāruṇyāṃ vātāyanasamanvitam 
samitkuśendhanasthānamāyudhānāṃ ca nairṛte  GarP 
abhyāgatālayaṃ ramyasaśayyāsanāpadukam 
toyāgnidīpasadbhṛtyairyuktaṃ dakṣiṇato bhavet  GarP 
gṛhāntarāṇi sarvāṇi sajalaiḥ kadalīgṛhaiḥ 
pañcavarṇaiśca kusumaiḥ śobhitāni prakalpayet  GarP 
prākāraṃ tadvahirdadyātpañcahastapramāṇataḥ 
evaṃ viṣṇvāśramaṃ kuryādvanaiścopavanairyutam  GarP 
catuḥ ṣaṣṭipado vāstuḥ prāsādādau prapūjitaḥ 
madhye catuṣpado brahmā dvipa dāstvaryamādayaḥ  GarP 
karṇe caivātha śikhyādyāstathā devāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
tebhyo hyubhayataḥ sārdhādanye 'pi dvipadāḥ surāḥ  GarP 
catuḥ ṣaṣṭipadā devā ityevaṃ parikīrtitāḥ 
carakī ca vidārī ca pūtanā pāparākṣasī  GarP 
īśānādyāstato bāhye devādyā hetukādayaḥ 
haitukastripurāntaśca agnivetālakau yamaḥ  GarP 
agnijihvaḥ kālakaśca karālo hyakapādakaḥ 
aiśānyāṃ bhīmarūpastu pātāle pretanāyakaḥ  GarP 
ākāśe gandhamālī syātkṣetrapālāṃstato yajet 
vistārābhihataṃ dairghyaṃ rāśiṃ vāstostu kārayet  GarP 
kṛtvā ca vasubhirbhāgaṃ śeṣaṃ baddhā yamādiśet 
punarguṇitamaṣṭābhirṛbhāgaṃ tu bhājayet  GarP 
yaccheṣaṃ tadbhavedṛkṣaṃ bhāgairhṛtvāvyayaṃ bhavet 
ṛkṣaṃ caturguṇaṃ kṛtvā navabhirbhāgahāritam  GarP 
śeṣamaṃśaṃ vijānīyāddevalasya mataṃ yathā 
aṣṭābhirguṇitaṃ piṇḍaṃ ṣaṣṭibhirbhāgāharitam  GarP 
yaccheṣaṃ tadbhavejjīvaṃ maraṇaṃ bhatahāritam 
vāstukroḍe gṛhaṃ kuryānna pṛṣṭhe mānavaḥ sadā  GarP 
vāmapārśvena svāpiti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
siṃhakanyātulāyāṃ ca dvāraṃ śudhyedathottaram  GarP 
evaṃ ca vṛścikādau syātpūrvadakṣiṇapaścimam 
dvāraṃ dīrghārdhavistāraṃ dvārāṇyaṣṭau smṛtāni ca  GarP 
santānapreṣyanīcatvaṃ svayānaṃ svarṇabhūṣaṇam 
sutahīnaṃ tu raudreṇa vīryaghnaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā  GarP 
vahnau badhaścāyurvṛddhiṃputtralābhasutṛptidaḥ 
dhanade nṛpapīḍādamarthaghnaṃ rogadaṃ jale  GarP 
nṛpabhī tirmṛtāpatyaṃ hyanapatyaṃ na vairadam 
arthadaṃ cārthahānyai ca doṣadaṃ putramṛtyudam  GarP 
dvārāṇyuttarasaṃjñāni pūrvadvārāṇi vacmyaham 
agnibhītirbahu kanyādhanasaṃmānakopadam  GarP 
rājaghnaṃ kopadaṃ pūrve phalato dvāramīritam 
īśānādau bhavetpūrvamagneyyādau tu dakṣiṇam  GarP 
nairṛtyādau paścimaṃ syādvāyavyādau tu cottaram 
aṣṭabhāge kṛte bhāge dvārāṇāṃ ca phalāphalam  GarP 
aśvatthaplakṣanyagrodhāḥ pūrvādau syādudumbaraḥ 
gṛhasya śobhanaḥ prokta īśāne caiva sālmaliḥ 
pūjito vignahārī syātprāsādasya gṛhasya ca  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe vāstumānalakṣaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
prāsādānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ ca vakṣye śaunaka tacchṛṇu 
catuḥ ṣaṣṭipadaṃ kṛtvā digvidikṣūpalakṣitam  GarP 
catuṣkoṇaṃ caturbhiśca dvārāṇi sūryasaṃkhyayā 
catvāriṃśāṣṭabiścaiva bhittīnāṃ kalpanā bhavet  GarP 
ūrdhvakṣetrasamā jaṅghā jaṅghārdhadviguṇaṃ bhavet 
garbhavistāravistīrṇaḥ śukāṅghriśca vidhīyate  GarP 
tattribhāgena kartavyaḥ pañcabhāgena vā punaḥ 
nirgamastu śukāṅghreśca ucchrāyaḥ śikharārdhagaḥ  GarP 
caturdhā śikharaṃ kṛtvā tribhāge vedibandhanam 
caturthe punarasyaiva kaṇṭhamāmūlasādhanam  GarP 
atha vāpi samaṃ vāstuṃ kṛtvā ṣoḍaśabhāgikam 
tasya madhye caturbhāgamādau garbhaṃ tu kārayet  GarP 
caturbhāgena bhittīnāmucchrāyaḥ syātpramāṇataḥ  GarP 
dviguṇaḥ śikharocchrāyo bhittyucchāyācca mānataḥ 
śikharārdhasya cairdhena vidheyāstu pradakṣiṇāḥ  GarP 
caturdikṣu tathā jñeyo nirgamastuḥ tathā budhaiḥ 
pañcabhāgena saṃbhajya garbhamānaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ  GarP 
bhāgamekaṃ gṛhītvā tu nirgamaṃ klapayetpunaḥ 
garbhasūtrasamo bhāgādagrato mukhamaṇḍapaḥ  GarP 
etatsāmānyamuddiṣṭaṃ prāsādasya hi lakṣaṇam 
liṅgamānamatho vakṣye pīṭho liṅgasamo bhavet  GarP 
dviguṇena bhavedrarbhaḥ samantācchaunaka dhruvam 
taddvidhā ca bhavedbhītirjaṅghā tadvistarārdhagā  GarP 
dviguṇaṃ śikharaṃ proktaṃ jaṅghāyāścaiva śaunaka 
pīṭhagarbhāvaraṃ karma tanmānena śukāṅghrikam  GarP 
nir gamastu samākhyātaḥ śeṣaṃ pūrvavadeva tu 
liṅgamānaṃ smṛtaṃ hyetaddvāramānamathocyate  GarP 
karāgraṃ vedavatkṛtvā dvāraṃ bhāgāṣṭamaṃ bhavet 
vistareṇa samākhyātaṃ dviguṇaṃsvecchayā bhavet  GarP 
dvāravatpīṭhamadhye tu śeṣaṃ suṣirakaṃ bhavet 
pādikaṃ śeṣikaṃ bhittirdvārārdhena parigrahāt  GarP 
tadvistārasamā jaṅghā sikharaṃ dviguṇaṃ bhavet 
śukāṅghriḥ pūrvavajjñeyā nirgamocchrāyakaṃ bhavet  GarP 
maṇḍape mānametattu svarūpaṃ cāparaṃ vade 
traivedaṃ kārayetkṣetraṃ yatra tiṣṭhanti devatāḥ  GarP 
itthaṃ kṛtena mānena bāhyabhāgavinirgatam 
nemiḥ pādena vistīrṇā prāsādasya samantataḥ  GarP 
garbhaṃ tu dviguṇaṃ kuryānnemyā mānaṃ bhavediha 
sa eva bhitterutsedho śikharo dviguṇo mataḥ  GarP 
prāsādānāṃ ca vakṣyāmi mānaṃ yoniṃ ca mānataḥ 
vairājaḥ puṣpakākhyaśca kailāso mālikāhvayaḥ  GarP 
triviṣṭapaṃ ca pañcaite prāsādāḥ sarvayonayaḥ 
prathamaścaturaśro hi dvitīyastu tadāyataḥ  GarP 
vṛtto vṛttāyataścānyo 'ṣṭāśraśceha ca pañcamaḥ 
etebhya eva sambhūtāḥ prāsādāḥ sumanoharāḥ  GarP 
sarvaprakṛtibhūtebhyaścatvāriṃśattathaiva ca 
meruśca mandaraścaiva vimānaśca tathāparaḥ  GarP 
bhadrakaḥ sarvatā bhadro rucako nandanastathā 
nandivardhanasaṃjñaśca śrīvatsaśca navetyamī  GarP 
caturaśrāḥ samudbhūtā vairājāditi gamyatām 
valabhī gṛharājaśca śā lāgṛhaṃ ca mandiram  GarP 
vimānaṃ ca tathā brahmamandiraṃ bhavanaṃ tathā 
uttambhaṃ śibikā veśma navaite puṣpakodbhavāḥ  GarP 
valayo dundubhiḥ padmo mahāpadmastathāparaḥ 
mukulī cāsya uṣṇīṣī śaṅkhaśca kalaśastathā  GarP 
guvāvṛkṣastathānyaśca vṛttāḥ kailāsasambhavāḥ 
gajo 'tha vṛṣabho haṃso garuḍaḥ siṃhanāmakaḥ  GarP 
bhūmukho bhūdharaścaiva śrījayaḥ pṛthivīdharaḥ 
vṛttāyatāḥ samudbhūtā navaite maṇikāhvayāt  GarP 
vajraṃ cakraṃ tathānyacca muṣṭikaṃ vabhrusaṃjñitam 
vakraḥ svastikakhaḍgau ca gadā śrīvṛkṣa eva ca  GarP 
vijayo nāmataḥ śvetastriviṣṭipasamudbhavāḥ 
trikoṇaṃ padmamardhenduścatuṣkoṇaṃ dviraṣṭakam  GarP 
yatra tatra vidhātavyaṃ saṃsthānaṃ maṇḍapasya tu 
rājyaṃ ca vibhavaścaivaḥ hyāyurvardvanameva ca  GarP 
putralābhaḥ striyaḥ puṣṭistrikoṇādikramādbhavet 
kuryāddhajādikaṃ khyātadvāri garbhagṛhaṃ tathā  GarP 
maṇāḍapaḥ samasaṃkhyābhirguṇitaḥ sūtrakastathā 
maṇḍapasya caturthāṃśādbhadraḥ kāryo vijānatā  GarP 
spardhāgavākṣakopeto nirgavākṣo 'tha vā bhavet 
sārdhabhittipramāṇena bhitimānena vā punaḥ  GarP 
bhitterdvaiguṇyato vāpi kartavyā maṇḍapāḥ kracit 
prāsāde mañcarī kāryā citrā viṣamabhūmikā  GarP 
parimāṇavirodhena rekhāvaiṣamyabhūṣitā 
ādhārastu caturdhāraścaturmaṇḍapaśobhitaḥ  GarP 
śataśṛṅgasamāyukto meruḥ prāsāda uttamaḥ 
maṇḍapāstasya kartavyā bhadraistribhiralaṅkṛtāḥ  GarP 
ghacanākāramānānāṃ bhinnābhinnā bhavanti te 
kiyanto yeṣu cādhārā nirādhārāśca kecana  GarP 
praticchandakabhedena prāsādāḥ sambhavanti te 
anyonyāsaṃkarāsteṣāṃ ghaṭanānāmabhedataḥ  GarP 
devatānāṃ viśeṣāya prāsādā bahavaḥ smṛtāḥ 
prāsāde niyamo nāsti devatānāṃ svayambhuvām  GarP 
tāneva devatānāṃ ca pūrvamānena kārayet 
caturaśrāyatāstattra catuṣkoṇasamanvitāḥ  GarP 
candraśālānvitā kāryā bherīśikharasaṃyutā 
purato vāhanānāṃ ca kartavyā lagnaghu
maṇḍapāḥ  GarP 
nāṭyaśālā ca kartavyā dvāradeśasamāśrayā 
prasāde devatānāṃ ca kāryā dikṣu vidikṣvapi  GarP 
dvārapālāśca kartavyā mukhyā gatvā pṛthakpṛthak 
kiñcidadūrataḥ kāryā maṭhāstatropajīvinām  GarP 
prāvṛtā jagatī kāryā phalapuṣpajalānvitā 
prasādeṣu surāṃsthāpya pūjābhiḥ pūjayennaraḥ 
vāsudevaḥ sarvadevaḥ sarvabhāk tadgṛhādikṛt  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśe ācārakāṇḍe prāsādaliṅgamaṇḍapādilakṣaṇanirūpaṇaṃnāma saptacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
pratiṣṭhāṃ sarvadevānāṃ saṃkṣepeṇa vadāmyaham 
sutithyādau suramyāṃ ca pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayedguruḥ  GarP 
ṛtvigbhiḥ saha cācāryaṃ varayenmadhyadeśagam 
svaśākhoktavidhānena atha vā praṇavena tu  GarP 
pañcabhirbahubhirvātha kuryātpādyārghyameva ca 
mudrikābhistathā vastrairgandhamālyānulepanaiḥ  GarP 
mantranyāsaṃ guruḥ kṛtvā tataḥ karma samārabhet 
prāsādasyāgrataḥ kuryānmaṇḍapaṃ daśahastakam  GarP 
kuryāddvādaśahastaṃ vā stambhaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiryutam 
dhvajāṣṭakaiścaturhastāṃ madhye vediṃ ca kārayet  GarP 
nadīsaṃgamatīrātthāṃ vālukāṃ tatra dāpayet 
caturaśraṃ kārmukābhaṃ vartulaṃ kamalākṛti  GarP 
pūrvāditaḥ samārabhya kartavyaṃ kuṇḍapañcakam 
athavā caturaśrāṇi sarvāṇyetāni kārayet  GarP 
śāntikarmidhānena sarvakāmārthasiddhaye 
śiraḥ sthāne tu devasya ācāryo homamācaret  GarP 
aiśānyāṃ kecidicchanti upalipyāvaniṃ śubhām 
dvārāṇi caiva catvāri kṛtvā vai toraṇāntike  GarP 
nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthabailvapālāśakhādirāḥ 
toraṇāḥ pañcahastāśca vastrapuṣpādyalaṅkṛtāḥ  GarP 
nikhaneddhastamekakaṃ catvāraścaturo diśaḥ 
pūrvadvāre mṛgendraṃ tu hayarājaṃ tu dakṣiṇe  GarP 
paścime gopatirnāma suraśārdūlamuttare 
agnimīleti hi mantreṇa prathamaṃ pūrvato nyaset  GarP 
īṣetvetihi mantreṇa dakṣiṇasyāṃ dvitīyakam 
agnāyāhimantreṇa paścimasyāṃ tṛtīyakam  GarP 
śannodevīti mantreṇa uttarasyāṃ caturthakam 
pūrve ambudavatkāryā āgnoyyāṃ dhūmarūpiṇī  GarP 
yāmyāṃ vai kṛṣṇarūpā tu nairṛtyā śyāmalā dhūsarā bhavet 
vāruṇyāṃ pāṇḍurā jñeyā vāyavyāṃ pītavarṇikā  GarP 
uttare raktavarṇā tu śukleśī ca patākikā 
bahurūpā tathā madhye indravidyeti pūrvake  GarP 
āgniṃ saṃsuptimantreṇa yamonāgeti dakṣiṇe 
pūjyā rakṣohanoveti paścime uttare 'pi ca  GarP 
vāta ityabhiṣicyātha āpyāyasveti cottare 
tamīśānamataścaiva viṣṇornuketi madhyame  GarP 
kalaśau tu tato dvaudvau niveśyau toraṇāntike 
vastrayugmasamāyuktāścandanādyaiḥ svalaṅkṛtāḥ  GarP 
puṣpairvitānairbahulairādivarṇābhimantritāḥ 
dikpālāśca tataḥ pūjyāḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā  GarP 
trātāramindrabhantreṇa agnirmūrdheti cāpare 
asminvṛkṣa itaṃ caiva pracārīti parā smṛtā  GarP 
kiñcedadhātu ācatvābhitvādeti ca saptamī 
imārudreti dikyālānpūjayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ  GarP 
homadravyāṇi vāyavye kuryātsopaskarāṇi ca 
śaṅkhāñchāstroditāñchvetānnetrābhyāṃ vinyasedguruḥ  GarP 
ālokanena dravyāṇi śuddhiṃ yānti na saṃśayaḥ 
tdṛdayādīni cāṅgāni vyāhṛtipraṇavena ca  GarP 
astraṃ caiva samastānāṃ nyāso 'yaṃ sarvakāmikaḥ 
akṣatānviṣṭaraṃ caiva astreṇaivābhimantritān  GarP 
viṣṭareṇa spṛśedduvyānyāgamaṇḍapasaṃbhṛtān 
akṣatānvikiretpaścādastrapūtānsamantataḥ  GarP 
śakrīṃ diśamathārabhya yāvadīśānagocaram 
avakīryākṣatārnsaṃvāṃllepayenmaṇḍapaṃ tataḥ  GarP 
gandhādyairarghyapātre ca mantragrāmaṃ nyasedguruḥ 
tenārghyapātratoyena prokṣayedyāgamaṇḍapam  GarP 
pratiṣṭhā yasya devasya tadākhyaṃ kalaśaṃ nyaset 
aiśānyāṃ pūjayedyāmye astreṇaiva ca bardhanīm  GarP 
kalaśaṃ vardhanīṃ caiva grahānvāsttoṣpatiṃ tathā 
āsanetāni sarvāṇi praṇavākhyaṃ japedguruḥ  GarP 
sūtragrīvaṃ ratnagarbhaṃ vastrayugmena veṣṭitam 
sarvauṣadhīgandhaliptaṃ pūjayetkalaśaṃ guruḥ  GarP 
devastu kalaśe pūjyo vardhanyā vastramuttamam 
vardhanyā tu samāyuktaṃ kalaśaṃ bhrāmayedanu  GarP 
vardhanīdhārayā siñcannagrato dhārayettataḥ 
abhyarcya vardhanīkumbhaṃ sthaṇḍile devamarcayet  GarP 
ghaṭaṃ cāvāhya vāyavyāṃ gaṇānāṃ tveti sadgaṇam 
devamīśānakoṇe tu japedvāstoṣpatiṃ budhaḥ  GarP 
vāstoṣpatīti mantreṇa vāstudoṣopaśāntaye 
kumbhasya pūrvato bhūtaṃ gaṇadevaṃ baliṃ haret  GarP 
paṭhediti ca vidyāśca kuryādālambhanaṃ budhaḥ 
yogeyogeti mantreṇāstaraṇaṃ śādvalaiḥ kuśaiḥ  GarP 
ṛtvigbhiḥ sārdhamācāryaḥ snānapīṭhe gurustadā 
vividhairbrahmaghoṣaiśca puṇyāhajayamaṅgalaiḥ  GarP 
kṛtvā brahmarathe devaṃ pratiṣṭhanti tato dvijāḥ 
aiśānyāmānayetpīṭhamaṇḍape vinyasedguruḥ  GarP 
bhadraṅkarṇetyatha snātvā sūtravalkalajena tu 
saṃsnāpya lakṣaṇoddhāraṃ kuryāttūryādi dūrābhi
vādanaiḥ  GarP 
madhusarpiḥ samāyuktaṃ kāṃsye vā tāmrabhājane 
akṣiṇī cāñjayeccāsya suvarṇasya śalākayā  GarP 
agnirjyotīti mantreṇa netrodvāṭaṃ tu kārayet 
lakṣaṇe kriyamāṇe tu nāmaikaṃ sthāpako vada det  GarP 
imaṃmegaṅgemantreṇa netrayoḥ śītalakriyā 
agnirmūrdheti mantreṇa dadyādvalmī kamṛttikām  GarP 
bilvodumbaramaśvatthaṃ vaṭaṃ pālāśameva ca 
yajñāyajñeti mantreṇa dadyātpañcakaṣāyakam  GarP 
pañcagavyaṃ snāpayecca sahadevyādi bhistataḥ 
sahadevī balā caiva śatamūlī śatāvarī  GarP 
kumārī ca guḍūcī ca siṃhī vyāghrī tathaiva ca 
yā oṣadhīti mantreṇa snānamoṣadhimajjalaiḥ  GarP 
yāḥ phalinīti mantreṇa phalasnānaṃ vidhīyate 
drupadādiveti mantreṇa kāryamudvartanaṃ budhaiḥ  GarP 
kalaśeṣu ca vinyasya uttarādiṣvanukramāt 
ratnāni caiva dhānyāni oṣadhīṃ śatapuṣpikām  GarP 
samudrāṃścaiva vinyasya caturaścaturo diśaḥ 
kṣīraṃ dadhi kṣīrodasya ghṛtodasyeti vā punaḥ  GarP 
āpyāyasva dadhikrāvṇo yā auṣadhīritīti ca 
tejo 'sīti ca mantraiśca kumbhaṃ caivābhimantrayet  GarP 
samudrākhyaiścaturbhiśca snāpayetkalaśaiḥ punaḥ 
snātaścaiva suveṣaśca dhūpo deyaśca gugguluḥ  GarP 
abhiṣekāya kumbheṣu tattattīrthāni vinyaset 
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni saritaḥ sāgarāstathā  GarP 
yā oṣadhīti mantreṇa kumbhaṃ caivābhimantrayet 
tena toyena yaḥ snāyātsa mucyetsarvapātakaiḥ  GarP 
abhiṣicya samudraiśca tvarghyaṃ dadyāttataḥ punaḥ 
gandhadvāreti gandhaṃ ca nyāsaṃ vai vedamantrakaiḥ  GarP 
svaśāstravihitaiḥ prāptairyuvaṃvastreti vastrakam 
kavihāviti mantreṇa ānayenmaṇḍapaṃ śubham  GarP 
śambhavāyeti mantreṇa śayyāyāṃ viniveśayet 
viśvataścakṣurmantreṇa kuryātsakalaniṣkalam  GarP 
sthitvā caiva pare tattve mantranyāsaṃ tu kārayet 
svaśāstravihito mantro nyāsastasmiṃstathoditaḥ  GarP 
vastreṇācchādayitvā tu pūjanīyaḥ svabhāvataḥ 
yathāśāstraṃ nivedyāni pādamūle tu dāpayet  GarP 
atha praṇavasaṃyuktaṃ vastrayugmena veṣṭitam 
kalaśaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ ca śiraḥ sthāne nivedayet  GarP 
sthitvā kuṇḍasamīpe 'tha agneḥ sthāpanamācaret 
svaśāstravihitairmantrairvedoktairvātha vā guruḥ  GarP 
śrīsūktaṃ pāvamānyaṃ ca vāsadāmyasavājinam 
vṛṣākapiṃ ca mitraṃ bahvacaḥ pūrvato japet  GarP 
rudraṃ puruṣasūktaṃ ca ślokādhyāyaṃ ca śukriyam 
brahmāṇaṃ pitṛmaitraṃ ca adhvaryurdakṣiṇe japet  GarP 
vedavrataṃ vāmadevyaṃ jyeṣṭhasāma rathantaram 
bheruṇḍāni ca sāmāni chandogaḥ paścime japet  GarP 
atharvaśirasaṃ caiva kumbhasūktamatharvaṇaḥ 
nīlarudrāṃśca maitraṃ ca atharvaścottare japet  GarP 
kuṇḍaṃ cāstreṇa saṃprokṣya ācāryastu viśeṣataḥ 
tāmrapātre śarāve vā yathāvibhavato 'pi vā  GarP 
jātavedasamānīya agratastaṃ niveśayet

amṛtīkṛtya taṃ paścānmantraiḥ sarvaiśca deśikaḥ 
pātraṃ gṛhya karābhyāṃ ca kuṇḍaṃ bhrāmya tataḥ punaḥ  GarP 
vaiṣṇavena tu yogena paraṃ tejastu niḥ kṣipet 
dakṣiṇe sthāpayedbrahma praṇītāñcottareṇa tu  GarP 
sādhāraṇena mantreṇa svasūtravihitena vā

ācāryāḥ kecidicchanti jātakarmādyanantaram 
pavitraṃ tu tataḥ kṛtvā kuryādājyasya saṃskṛtim  GarP 
ācāryo 'tha nirīkṣyāpi nīrājyamabhimantritam 
ājyabhāgābhighārāntamavekṣetājyasiddhaye  GarP 
pañcapañcāhutīrhutvā ājyena tadanantaram 
garbhādhānāditastāvadyāvadgaudānikaṃ bhavet  GarP 
svaśāstravihitairmantraiḥ praṇavenātha homayet 
tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ dattvā pūrṇātpūrṇamanārethaḥ  GarP 
evamutpādito vahniḥ sarvakarmasu siddhidaḥ 
pūjayitvā tato vahniṃ kuṇḍeṣu viharettathā  GarP 
indrādīnāṃ svamantraiśca tathāhutiśataṃśatam 
purṇāhutiṃ śatasyānte sarveṣāṃ caiva homayet  GarP 
svāmāhutimathājyeṣu hotā tatkalaśe nyaset 
devatāścaiva mantrāṃśca tathaiva jātavedasam  GarP 
ātmānamekataḥ kṛtvā tataḥ pūrṇāṃ pradāpayet

caturthau juhuyātpaścādyajamānaḥ samāhitaḥ

śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam

narte hyārādhanātpuṇyaṃ vidyate karma vaidikam  GarP 
tasmāttatrādimadhyānte cetasā dhārayeddharim 
tadviṣṇoriti mantreṇa sūktena puruṣeṇa tu  GarP 
nivedayecca ātmānaṃ viṣṇave 'malatejase 
tadādhyātmamanāḥ śāntastadviṣṇoriti mantrataḥ  GarP 
aprete saśirā vetiyajetvā puṣpake harim 
devayajñaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ tathaiva ca 
mānuṣaṃ brahmayajñaṃ ca pañca yajñānsamācaret  GarP 
yadi syāttarpaṇādarvāgbrayajñaṃ kuto bhavet 
kṛtvā manuṣyayajñaṃ vai tataḥ svādhyāyamācaret  GarP 
vaiśvadevastu kartavyo devayajñaḥ sa tu smṛtaḥ 
bhūtayajñaḥṛ sa vai jñeyo bhūtebhyo yastvayaṃ baliḥ  GarP 
śvabhyaśca śvapacebhyaśca patitādibhya eva ca 
dadyādbhūmau bahistvannaṃ pakṣibhyaśca dvijottamaḥ  GarP 
ekaṃ tu bhojayedvipraṃ pitṝnuddiśya sattamāḥ 
nityaśrāddhaṃ taduddiśya pitṛyajño gatipradaḥ  GarP 
uddhṛtya vā yathāśakti kiñcidannaṃ samāhitaḥ 
vedatattvārthaviduṣe dvijāyaivopapādayet  GarP 
pūjayedatithiṃ nityaṃ namasyedarcayoddvijam 
manovākkarmabhiḥ śāntaṃ svāgataiḥ svagṛhaṃ tataḥ  GarP 
bhikṣāmāhurgrāsamātramannaṃ tatsyāccaturguṇam 
puṣkalaṃ hantakāraṃ tu taccaturguṇamucyate  GarP 
godohamātrakālaṃ vai pratīkṣyo hyatithiḥ svayam 
abhyāgatānyathāśakti pūjayedatithiṃ tathā  GarP 
bhikṣāṃ vai bhikṣave dadyādvidhivadbrahyacāriṇe 
dadyādannaṃ yathāśakti arthibhyo lobhavarjitaḥ  GarP 
bhuñjati bandhubhiḥ sārdhaṃ vāgyato 'nnamakutsayan 
akṛtvā tu dvijaḥ pañca mahāyajñān dvijottamaḥ  GarP 
bhuñjate cetsa mūḍhātmā tiryagyoniṃ ca gacchati 
vedābhyāso 'nvahaṃ śaktyā mahāyajñakriyākṣamāḥ  GarP 
nāśayantyāśu pāpāni devānāmarcanaṃ tathā 
yo mohādatha vālasyādakṛtvā devatārcanam  GarP 
bhuṅkte sa yāti narakāntsūṃkareṣveva jāyate 
aśaucaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi aśuciḥ pātakī sadā  GarP 
aśaucaṃ caiva saṃsargācchuddhiḥ saṃsargavarjanāt 
daśāhaṃ prāhurāśaucaṃ sarveviprā vipaścitaḥ  GarP 
mṛteṣu vātha jāteṣu brāhmaṇānāṃ dvijottama 
ādantajananāt sadya ācūḍādekarātrakam  GarP 
trirātramaupanayanāddaśarātramataḥ param 
kṣattriyo dvādaśahena daśabhiḥ pañcabhirviśaḥ  GarP 
śudhyenmāsena vai śūdro yatīnāṃ nāsti pātakam 
rātribhirmāsatulyābhirgarbhastrāveṣu śaucakam  GarP 
iti gāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe nityakarmāśaucayornirūpaṇaṃ nāma pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
brahmovāca 
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dānadharmamanuttamam 
arthānāmucite pātre śraddhayā pratipādanam  GarP 
dānaṃ tu kathitaṃ tajjñairbhuktimuktiphalapradam 
nyāyenopārjayedvittaṃ dānabhogaphalaṃ ca tat  GarP 
adhyāpanaṃ yājanaṃ ca vṛttamāhuḥ pratigraham 
kusīdaṃ kṛṣivāṇijyaṃ kṣattravṛtto 'tha varjayet  GarP 
yaddīyate tu pātrebhyastaddānaṃ parikīrtitam 
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ vimalaṃ dānamīritam  GarP 
ahanyahani yatkiñciddīyate 'nupakāriṇe 
anuddiśya phalaṃ tasmādbrāhmaṇāya tu nityaśaḥ  GarP 
yattu pāpopaśāntyai ca dīyate vidupāṃ kare 
naimittikaṃ taduddiṣṭandānaṃ sadbhiranuṣṭhitam  GarP 
apatyavijayaiśvaryasvargārthaṃ yatpradīyate 
dānaṃ tatkāmyamākhyātamṛṣibhirdharmācintakaiḥ  GarP 
īśvaraprīṇanārthāya brahmāvitsupradīyate 
cetasā sattvayuktena dānaṃ tadvimalaṃ śivam  GarP 
ikṣubhiḥ santatāṃ bhumiṃ yavagodhūmaśālinīm 
dadāti vedaviduṣe sa na bhūyo 'bhijāyate  GarP 
bhūmidānātparaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati 
vidyāṃ dattvā brāhmaṇāya brahmaloke mahīyate  GarP 
dadyādaharahastāstu śraddhayā brahmacāriṇe 
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmasthānamavāpnuyāt  GarP 
vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ tu brāhmaṇānsapta pañca ca 
upoṣyābhyarcayedvidvānmadhunā tilasarpiṣā  GarP 
gandhādibhiḥ samabhyarcya vācayedvā svayaṃ vadet 
prīyatāṃ dharmarājeti yathā manasi vartate  GarP 
yāvajjīvaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva naśyati 
kṛṣṇājine tilānkṛtvā hiraṇyamadhusarpiṣā  GarP 
dadāti yastu viprāya sarvaṃ tarati duṣkṛtam 
ghṛtānnamudakaṃ caiva vaiśākhyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ  GarP 
nirdiśya dharmarājāya viprebhyo mucyate bhayāt 
dvādaśyāmarcayedviṣṇumupoṣyāghapraṇāśanam  GarP 
sarvapāpavinirmukto naro bhavati niścitam 
yo hi yāṃ devatāmicchetsamārādhayituṃ naraḥ  GarP 
brāhmaṇānpūjayeddatnādbhojayedyoṣitaḥ surān 
santānakāmaḥ satataṃ pūjayedvai purandaram  GarP 
brahmavarcasakāmastu brāhmaṇānbrahmaniścayāt 
ārogyakāmo 'tha raviṃ dhanakāmo hutāśanam  GarP 
karmaṇāṃ siddhikāmastu pūjayedvai vināyakam 
bhogakāmo hi śaśinaṃ balakāmaḥ samīraṇam  GarP 
mumukṣuḥ sarvasaṃsārātprayatnenārcayeddharim 
akāmaḥ sarvakāmo vā pūjayettu gadādharam  GarP 
vāridastṛptimāpnoti sukhamakṣayyamannadaḥ 
tilapradaḥ prajāmiṣṭāṃ dīpadaścakṣuruttamam  GarP 
bhūmidaḥ sarvamāpnoti dīrghamāyurhiraṇyadaḥ 
gṛhado 'gryāṇi veśmāni rūpyado rūpamuttamam  GarP 
vāsodaścāndrasālokyamaśvisālokyamaśvadaḥ 
anaḍuddaḥ śriyaṃ puṣṭāṃ godo bradhnasya viṣṭapam  GarP 
yānaśayyāprado bhāryāmaiśvaryamabhayapradaḥ 
dhānyadaḥ śāvataṃ saukhyaṃ brahmado brahma śāśvatam  GarP 
vedavitsu dadajjñānaṃ svargaloke mahīyate 
gavāṃ ghāsapradānena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  GarP 
indhanānāṃ pradānena dīptāgnirjāyate naraḥ 
auṣadhaṃ snehamāhāraṃ rogirogapraśāntaye  GarP 
dadāno rogarahitaḥ sukhī dīrghāyureva ca 
asipatravanaṃ mārgaṃ kṣuradhārāsamanvitam  GarP 
tīkṣṇā tapaṃ ca taraticchatropānatprado naraḥ 
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ loke yaccāsya dayitaṃ gṛhe  GarP 
tattadguṇavate deyaṃ tadevākṣayamicchatā 
ayena viṣuve caiva grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ  GarP 
saṃkrāntyādiṣu kāleṣu dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam 
prayāgādiṣu tīrtheṣu gayāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ  GarP 
dānadharmātparo dharmo bhūtānāṃ nahe vidyate 
svargāyurbhūtikāmena dānaṃ pāpopaśāntaye  GarP 
dīyamānaṃ tu yo mohādgoviprāgnisureṣu ca 
nivārayati pāpātmā tiryagyoniṃ vrajennaraḥ  GarP 
yastu durbhikṣavelāyāmannādyaṃ na prayacchati 
mriyamāṇeṣu vipreṣu brahmahā sa tu garhitaḥ  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe dānadharmanirūpaṇaṃ nāmaikapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
brahmovāca 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittavidhiṃ dvijāḥ 
brahmahā ca surāpaśca steyī ca gurutalpagaḥ  GarP 
pañca pātakinastvete tatsaṃyogī ca pañcamaḥ 
upapāpāni gohatyāprabhṛtīni surā jaguḥ  GarP 
brahmahā dvādaśābdāni kuṭīṃ kṛtvā vane vaset 
kuryādanaśanaṃ vātha bhṛgoḥ patanameva ca  GarP 
jvalantaṃ vā viśedagniṃ jalaṃ vā praviśetsvayam 
brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā samyak prāṇānparityajet  GarP 
dattvā cānnaṃ ca viduṣe brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati 
aśvamedhāvabhṛthake snātvā vā mucyate dvijaḥ  GarP 
sarvasvaṃ vā vedavide brāhmaṇāya pradāpayet 
sarasvatyāstaraṅgiṇyāḥ saṅgame lokaviśrute  GarP 
śuddhe triṣavaṇasnātastrirātropoṣito dvijaḥ 
setubandhe naraḥ snātvā mucyate brahmahatyayā  GarP 
kapālamocane snātvā vārāṇasyāṃ tathaiva ca 
surāpastu surāṃ pītvā agnivarṇāṃ dvijottamaḥ  GarP 
payo ghṛtaṃ vā gomūtraṃ tasmātpāpātpramucyate 
suvarṇasteyī muktaḥ syānmusalena hato nṛpaiḥ  GarP 
cīravāsā dvijo 'raṇye caredbrahmahaṇavratam 
gurubhāryāṃ samāruhya brāhmaṇaḥ kāmamohitaḥ  GarP 
avagūhetstriyaṃ taptāṃ dīptāṃ kārṣṇāyasīṃ kṛtām 
gurvaṅganāgāminaśca careyurbahmahavratam  GarP 
cāndrāyaṇāni vā kuryātpañca catvāri vā punaḥ 
patitena ca saṃsargaṃ kurute yastu vai dvijaḥ  GarP 
sa tatpāpāpanodārthaṃ tasyaiva vratamācaret 
taptakṛcchraṃ caredvātha saṃvatsaramatandritaḥ  GarP 
sarvasvadānaṃ vidhivatsarvapāpaviśodhanam 
cāndrāyaṇaṃ ca vidhinā kṛtaṃ caivātikṛcchrakam  GarP 
puṇyakṣetre gayādau ca gamanaṃ pāpanāśanam 
amāvasyāṃ tithiṃ prāpya yaḥ samārādhayedbhavam  GarP 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
upoṣitaścaturdaśyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe samāhitaḥ  GarP 
yamāya dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca 
vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtakṣayāya ca  GarP 
pratyekaṃ tilasaṃyuktāndadyātsapta jalāñjalīn 
snātvā nadyāṃ tu pūrvāhne mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  GarP 
brahmacaryamadhaḥ śayyāmupavāsaṃ dvijārcanam 
vrateṣveteṣu kurvīta śāntaḥ saṃyatamānasaḥ  GarP 
paṣṭhyāmupoṣito devaṃ śuklapakṣe samāhitaḥ 
saptamyāmarcayedbhānuṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  GarP 
ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāraḥ samabhyarcya janārdanam 
dvādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣasya mahāpāpaiḥ pramucyate  GarP 
tapo japastīrthasevā devabrāhmaṇapūjanam 
grahaṇādiṣu kāleṣu mahāpātakanāśanam  GarP 
yaḥ sarvapāpayukto 'pi puṇyatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ 
niyamena tyajetprāṇānmucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  GarP 
brahmaghnaṃ vā kṛtaghnaṃ vā mahāpātakadūṣitam 
bhartāramuddharennārī praviṣṭā saha pāvakam  GarP 
pativratā tu yā nārī bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇotsukā 
na tasyā vidyate pāpamiha loke paratra ca  GarP 
tathā rāmasya subhagā sītā trailokyaviśrutā 
patnī dāśaratherdevī vijigye rākṣaseśvaram  GarP 
phalgutīrthādiṣu snātaḥ sarvācāraphalaṃ labhet 
ityāha bhagavānviṣṇuḥ purā mama yatavratāḥ  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe prāyaścittanirūpaṇaṃ nāma dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
evaṃ brahmābravīcchrutvā hareraṣṭanidhīṃstathā 
tatra padmamahāpadmau tathā makarakacchapau  GarP 
mukundakuna
ndau nīlaśca śaṅkhaścaivāparo nidhiḥ 
satyāmṛddhau bhavantyete svarūpaṃ kathayāmyaham  GarP 
padmena lakṣitaścaiva sāttviko jāyate naraḥ 
dākṣiṇyasāraḥ puruṣaḥ suvarṇādikasaṃgraham  GarP 
rupyādi kuryāddadyāttu yatidaivādiyajvanām 
mahāpadmāṅkito dadyāddhanādyaṃ dhārmikāya ca  GarP 
nīdhī padmamahāpadmau sāttvikau puruṣau smṛtī 
makareṇāṅkitaḥ khaḍgabāṇakuntādisaṃgrahī  GarP 
dadyācchrutāya maitrīṃ ca yāti nityaṃ ca rājabhiḥ 
dravyārthaṃ śatruṇā nāśaṃ saṃgrāme cāpi saṃvrajet  GarP 
makaraḥ kacchapaścaiva tāmasau tu nidhī smṛtau 
kacchapī viśvasennaiva na bhuṅkena nā
dadāti ca  GarP 
nidhānamurvyāṃ kurute nidhiḥ sopyekapūruṣaḥ 
rājasenamukundena lakṣitā rājyasaṃgrahī  GarP 
bhuktabhogo gāyanebhyo dadyādveśyādikāsu ca 
rajastamomayo nandī ādhāraḥ syātkulasya ca  GarP 
stutaḥ prīto bhavati vai bahubhāryā bhavanti ca 
pūrvamitreṣu śaithilyaṃ prītimanyaiḥ karoti ca  GarP 
nīlana cāṅkitaḥ sattvatejasā saṃyuto bhavet 
vastradhānyādisaṃgrāhī taḍāgādi karoti ca  GarP 
tripūpau ruṣo nidhiścaiva āmrārāmādi kārayet 
ekasya syānnidhiḥ śaṅkhaḥ svayaṃ bhuṅkte dhanādintakam  GarP 
kadannabhukparijano na ca śobhanavastradhṛk 
svapoṣaṇaparaḥ śaṅkhī dadyātparanare vṛthā  GarP 
miśrāvalokanānmiśrasvabhāvaphaladāyinaḥ 
nidhīnāṃ rūpamuktaṃ tu hariṇāpi harādike 
harirbhuvanakośādi yathovāca tathā vade  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe navanidhivarṇanaṃ nāma tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ

hariruvāca 
agnīdhraścāgnibāhuśca bapuṣmāndhyutimāṃstathā

jātismarā mahābhāgā nairājyāya mamo daṣuḥ 
vibhajya sapta dvīpāni saptānāṃ pradadau nṛpaḥ  GarP 
yojanānāṃ pramāṇena pañcāśatkoṭirāplutā

pratīhāraścatatputraḥ pratihartā tadātmajaḥ  GarP

 iti śrāgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe bhuvanakośavarṇanopayogipriyavratavaṃśanirūpaṇaṃ nāma catuḥ pañcaśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ

hariruvāca 
madhye tvilāvṛto varṣo bhadrāśvaḥ pūrvato 'dbhutaḥ 
pūrvadakṣaiṇato varṣo hiraṇvānvṛṣabhadhvaja  GarP 
tataḥ kimpuruṣo varṣo merordakṣiṇataḥ smṛtaḥ

siddhiḥ svābhāvikī rudra 
varjayitvā tu bhāratam 
indradvīpaḥ kaśerumāṃstāmravarṇo gabhastitamān  GarP 
nāgadvīpaḥ kaṭāhaśca siṃhalo vāruṇastathā

andhrā dakṣiṇato rudra

pradeśinīgatā rekhā kaniṣṭhāmūlagāminī  GarP 
śatāyuṣaṃ ca kurute chinnayā taruto bhayam

māṃsalaiśca dhanopetā āraktairadharairnṛpāḥ 
bimbopamaiśca sphuṭitairoṣṭhairūkṣaiścakaṇḍitaiḥ  GarP 
viṣamairdhanahīnāśca dantāḥ snigdhā ghanāḥ śubhāḥ

ślakṣṇā dīrghā ca vijñeyā tālū śvete dhanakṣaye 
kṛṣṇe ca paruṣo vakraṃ samaṃ saumyaṃ ca saṃvṛtam  GarP 
bhūpānāmamalaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ viparītaṃ ca duḥ khinām 
mahā duḥ khaṃ durbhagāṇāṃ strīmukhaṃ putramāpnuyāt  GarP 
āḍhyānāṃ vartulaṃ vakraṃ nirdravyāṇāṃ ca dīrghakam

vakrāntaiḥ padmapatrābhairlocanaiḥ sukhabhāginaḥ

annatairvipulaiḥ śaṅkhairlalāṭairviṣamaistathā  GarP

puṃsaḥ syādativistīrṇaṃ lalāṭaṃ vadanaṃ hyuraḥ

svalpāyuṣo bahu laghu
cchinnā dīrghāchinnā mahāyuṣam

vāmāvartaṃ nimnamalpaṃ duḥ khitānāṃ ca guhyakam

pṛthulayā pracaṇḍāśca striyaḥ syurnātra saṃśayaḥ

śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
hariruvāca 
nirlakṣaṇā śubhā syācca cakrāṅkitaśilārcanāt

ata ūrdhvamanantaḥ syācchakre rekādikaiḥ kramāt 
sudarśanā lakṣitāśca pūjitāḥ sarvakāmadāḥ  GarP 
śālagrāmaśilā yatra devo dvāravatībhavaḥ 
ubhayoḥ saṃgamo yatra tatra muktirna saṃśayaḥ  GarP 
śālagrāmo dvārakā ca naimiṣaṃ puṣkaraṃ gayā

gaṅgā ca narmadā caiva candrabhāgā sarasvatī 
puruṣottamo mahākālastīrthānyetāni śaṅkara  GarP 
sarvapāpaharāṇyeva bhuktamuktipradāni vai 
prabhavo vibhavaḥ śuklaḥ pramodo 'tha prajāpatiḥ  GarP 
aṅgirāḥ śrīmukho bhāvaḥ yuvā dhātā tathaiva ca 
īśvaro bahudhānyaśca pramāthī vikramo viṣuḥ  GarP 
citrabhānuḥ svabānuśca tāraṇaḥ pārthivo vyayaḥ

nandano vijayaścaiva jayo manmathadurmukhau 
hemalambo vilaṃbaśca vikāraḥ śarvarī plavaḥ  GarP 
śubhakṛcchobhanaḥ krodhī viśvāvamuparābhavau

paridhāvī pramādī ca ānando rākṣaso nalaḥ

udāsāmṛtyupīḍāśca kujaḥ somasutaḥ kramāt  GarP 
guruśukrau ca mandaśca ravicandrau yathoditam

 iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe jyotiḥ śāstre śālagrāmaṣaṣṭyūbdasvarodayānāṃ nirūpaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

iti jyotiḥ śāstraṃ samāptam 
sūta uvāca 
hareḥ śrutvā haro gaurīṃ dehasthaṃ jñānamabravīt  GarP 
kujo vahnī raviḥ pṛthvī saurirāpaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
vāyusaṃsthāsthito rāhurdakṣarandhrāvabhāsakaḥ  GarP 
guruḥ śukrastathā saumyaścandraścaiva caturthakaḥ 
vāmanāḍīṃ tu madhyasthāṃ kārayedātmanastathā  GarP 
yadācara ilāyuktastadā karmasamācaret 
sthānasevāṃ tathā dhyānaṃ vāṇijyaṃ rājadarśanam  GarP 
anyāni śubhakarmāṇi kārayeta prayatnataḥ 
dakṣanāḍīpravāhe tu śanirbhaumaśca saihikaḥ  GarP 
inaścaiva tathāpye pāpānāmudayo bhavet 
śubhāśubhaviveko hi jñāyate tu svarodayāt  GarP 
dehamadhye sthitā nāḍyo bahurūpāḥ suvistarāḥ 
nābheradhastādyaḥ kandastvaṅkurāstatra nirgatāḥ  GarP 
dvisaptatisahasrāṇi nābhimadhye vyavasthite 
cakravacca sthitāstāstu sarvāḥ prāṇaharāḥ smṛtāḥ  GarP 
tāsāṃ madhye trayaḥ śreṣṭhā vāmadakṣaiṇamadhyamāḥ 
vāmā somātmikā proktā dakṣiṇā ravisannibhā  GarP 
madhyamā ca bhavedagniḥ phalantī kālapūriṇī 
vāmā hyamṛtarūpā ca jagadāpyāyane sthitā  GarP 
dakṣiṇā raudrabhāgena jagacchoṣayate sadā 
dvayorvāhe tu mṛtyuḥ syātsarvakāryavināśinī  GarP 
nirgame tu bhavedvāmā praveśe dakṣaiṇā smṛtā 
iḍācāre tathā saumyaṃ candrasūryagatastathā  GarP 
kārayetkrūra karmāṇi prāṇe piṅgalasaṃsthite 
yātrāyāṃ sarvakāryeṣu viṣāpahāraṇe iḍā  GarP 
bhojane maithune yuddhe piṅgalā siddhidāyikā 
uccāṭamāraṇādyeṣu karmasveteṣu piṅgalā  GarP 
maithune caiva saṃgrāme bhojane siddhidāyikā 
śobhaneṣu ca kāryeṣu yātrāyāṃ viṣakarmaṇi  GarP 
śāntimuktyarthasiddhyai ca iḍā yojyā narādhipaiḥ 
dvābhyāṃ caiva pravāhe ca krūrasaumyavivarjane  GarP 
viṣavattaṃ tu jānīyātsaṃsmarettu vicakṣaṇaḥ 
saumyādiśubhakāryeṣu lābhādijayajīvite  GarP 
gamanāgamane caiva vāmā sarvatra pūjitā 
yuddhādibhojane ghāte strīṇāṃ caiva tu saṃgame  GarP 
praśastā dakṣiṇā nāḍī praveśe kṣudrakarmaṇi 
śubhāśubhāni kāryāṇi lābhālābhau jayājayau  GarP 
jīvājīvāya yatpṛcchenna sidhyati ca madhyamā 
vāmācāre 'thavā dakṣe pratyaye yatra nāyakaḥ  GarP 
tanusthaḥ pṛcchate yastu tatra siddhirna saṃśayaḥ 
vaicchando vāmadevastu yadā vahati cātmani  GarP 
tatra bhāge sthitaḥ pṛcchetsiddhirbhavati niṣphalā 
vāme vā dakṣiṇe vāpi yatra saṃkramate śivā  GarP 
ghore ghorāṇi kāryāṇi saumye vai madhyamāni ca 
prasthite bhāgato haṃse dvābhyāṃ vai sarvavāhinī  GarP 
tadā mṛtyuṃ vijānīyādyogī yogaviśāradaḥ 
yatrayatra sthitaḥ pṛcchedvāmadakṣiṇasaṃmukhaḥ  GarP 
tatratatra samaṃ diśyādvātasyodayanaṃ sadā 
agrato vāmikā śreṣṭhā pṛṣṭhato dakṣiṇā śubhā  GarP 
vāmena vāmikā proktā dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇā śubhā 
vāme vāmā śubhe caiva dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇā śubhā  GarP 
jīvo jīvati jīvena yacchūnyaṃ tastvaro bhavet 
yatkiñcitkāryamuddiṣṭaṃ jayādiśubhalakṣaṇam  GarP 
tatsarvaṃ pūrṇanāḍyāṃ tu jāyate nirvikalpataḥ

vrīhibhirmardanīyaṃ vā śuṣkavastropaveṣṭitam  GarP 
yattu nāyāti vaivarṇyaṃ vijñeyaṃ tadakṛtrimam 
sitaṃ pramāṇavatsnigdhaṃ guru svacchaṃ sunirmalam  GarP 
tejo 'dhikaṃ suvṛttaṃ ca mauktikaṃ guṇavatsmṛtam  GarP 
pramāṇavadgauravaraśmiyuktaṃ sitaṃ suvṛttaṃ samasūkṣmavedham 
akreturapyāvahati pramodaṃ yanmauktikaṃ tadguṇavatpradiṣṭam  GarP 
evaṃ samastena guṇodayena yanmauktikaṃ yogamupāgataṃ syāt 
na tasya bhartāramanarthajāta eko 'pi kaścit samupaiti doṣaḥ  GarP 
 iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe muktāphalapramāṇādivarṇanaṃ nāma muktāphalaparīkṣā nāmaikonasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
divākarastasya mahāmahimno mahāsurasyottamaratnabījam 
asṛggṛhītvā carituṃ pratasthe nistriṃśanīlena nabhaḥ sthalena  GarP 
jettrā surāṇāṃ samareṣvajastraṃ vīryāvalepoddhatamānasena 
laṅkādhipenārdhapathe sametya svarbhānuneva prasabhaṃ niruddhaḥ  GarP 
tatsiṃhalīcārunitambabimbavikṣo bhitāgādhamahāhradāyām 
pūgadrumābaddhataṭadvayāyāṃ mumoca sūryaḥ sariduttamāyām  GarP 
tataḥ prabhṛti sā gaṅgā tulyapuṇyaphalodayā 
nāmnā rāvaṇagaṅgeti prathimānamupāgatā  GarP 
tataḥ prabhṛtyeva ca śarvarīṣu kūlāni ratnairnicitāni tasyāḥ 
suvarṇanārācaśatairivāntarbahiḥ pradīptairniśitāni bhānti  GarP 
tasyāstaṭepūjjvacārurāgā bhavanti toyeṣu ca padmarāgāḥ 
saugandhikotthāḥ kuruvindajāśca mahāguṇāḥ sphāṭikasaṃprasūtāḥ  GarP 
bandhū kaguñjāsakalendragopajavāsamāsṛksamavarṇaśobhāḥ 
bhrājiṣṇavo dāḍimabījavarṇāstathāpare kiśukapuṣpabhāsaḥ  GarP 
khindurapadmotpalakuṅkumānāṃ lākṣārasasyāpi samānavarṇaḥ 
sāṃdre 'pi rāge prabhayā svayaiva bhānti svalakṣyāḥ sphuṭamadhyaśobhāḥ  GarP 
bhānośca bhāsāmanuvedhayogāmāsādya raśami prakareṇa dūram 
pārśvāni sarvāṇyanurañjayanti guṇāpapannāḥ sphaṭikaprasūtāḥ  GarP 
kusuṃbhanīlavyatimiśrarāgapratyugraraktābujatulyabhāsaḥ 
tathāpare 'ruṣkarakaṇṭakāripuṣpatviṣo hiṅgulavattviṣo 'nye  GarP 
cakorapuṃskokilasārasānāṃ netrāvabhāsaśca bhavanti kecit 
anye punaḥ santi ca puṣpitānāṃ tulyatviṣā kokanadottamānām  GarP 
prabhāvakāṭhinyagurutvayogaiḥ prāyaḥ samānāḥ sphaṭikodbhavānām 
ānīlaraktotpalacārubhāsaḥ saugandhikotthā maṇayo bhavanti  GarP 
kāmaṃ tu rāgaḥ kuruvindajeṣu sa naiva yādṛk sphaṭikodbhaveṣu 
nirarciṣo 'ntarbahulā bhavanti prabhāvavanto 'pi nataiḥ samastaiḥ  GarP 
ye tu rāvaṇagaṅgāyāṃ jāyante kuruvindakāḥ 
padmarāgaghanaṃ rāgaṃ bibhrāṇāḥ sphaṭikārciṣaḥ  GarP 
varṇānuyāyinasteṣā māndhradeśe tathā pare 
na jāyante hi ye kecinmūlyaleśamavāpnuyuḥ  GarP 
tathaiva sphāṭikotthānāṃ deśe tumburusaṃjñake 
sadharmāṇaḥ prajāyante svalpamūlyā hi te smṛtāḥ  GarP 
varṇādhikyaṃ gurutvaṃ ca snigdhatā samatācchatā 
arciṣmattā mahattā ca maṇīnāṃ guṇasaṃgrahaḥ  GarP 
ye karkaracchidramalopadigdhāḥ prabhāvimuktāḥ paruṣā vivarṇāḥ 
na te praśastā maṇayo bhavanti samānato jātiguṇaiḥ samastaiḥ  GarP 
doṣopasṛṣṭaṃ maṇimaprabodhādvibharti yaḥ kaścana kañcideva 
taṃ śokacintāmayamṛtyuvittanāśādayo doṣagaṇā bhajante  GarP 
kāmaṃ cārutarāḥ pañca jātīnā pratirūpakāḥ 
vijā tayaḥ prayatnena vidvāṃstanupalakṣayet  GarP 
kalaśapurodbhavasiṃhalatumburudeśotthamuktapāṇīyāḥ 
śrīpūrṇakāśca sadṛśā vijātayaḥ padmarāgāṇām  GarP 
tuṣopasargātkalaśābhidhānamātāmrabhāvādapi tumburūttham 
kārṣṇyāttathā siṃhaladeśajātaṃ muktābhidhānaṃ nabhasaḥ svabhāvāt  GarP 
śrīpūrṇakaṃ dīptivinākṛtatvādvijātiliṅgāśraya eva bhedaḥ 
yastāmrikāṃ puṣyati padmarāgo yogāttuṣāṇāmiva pūrṇamadhyaḥ  GarP 
strehapradigdhaḥ pratibhāti yaśca yo vā praghṛṣṭaḥ prajahāti dīptim 
ākrāntamūrdhā ca tathāṅgulibhyāṃ yaḥ kālikāṃ pārśvagatāṃ bibharti  GarP 
saṃprāpya cotkṣipya yathānuvṛttiṃ vibhartiyaḥ sarvaguṇānatīva 
tulyapramāṇasya ca tulyajāteryo vā gurutvena bhavettu tulyaḥ 
prāpyāpi ratnākarajā svajātiṃ lakṣedgurutvena guṇena vidvān  GarP 
apraṇaśyati sandehe śāṇe tu parilekhayet 
susva jātakasamutthena likhitvāpi parasparam  GarP 
vajraṃ vā kuruvindaṃ vā vimucyānena kenacit 
nāśakyaṃ lekhanaṃ kartuṃ padmarāgendranīlayoḥ  GarP 
jātyasya sarve 'pi maṇerna jātu vijātayaḥ santi samānavarṇāḥ 
tathāpi nānākaraṇārthameva bhedaprakāraḥ paramaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ  GarP 
guṇopapannena sahāvabaddhomeṇirna dhāryo viguṇo hi jātyā 
na kaustubhenāpi sahāvabaddhaṃ vidvānvijātiṃ bibhṛyātkadācit  GarP 
cāṇḍāla eko 'pi yathā dvijātīnsametya bhūrīnapi hantyayatnāt 
atho maṇīnbhūriguṇopapannāñchakroti viplāvayituṃ vijātyaḥ  GarP 
sapatnamadhye 'pi kṛtādhivāsaṃ pramādavṛttāvapi vartamānam 
na padmarāgasya mahāguṇasya bhartāramāpatspṛśatīha kācit  GarP 
doṣopasargaprabhavāśca ye te nopadravāstaṃ samabhidravanti 
guṇaiḥ samuttejitacārurāgaṃ yaḥ padmarāgaṃ prayato bibharti  GarP 
vajrasya yattaṇḍulasaṃkhyayoktaṃ mūlyaṃ samutpāditagauravasya 
tatpadmarāgasya mahāguṇasya tanmāṣakalpākalitasya mūlyam  GarP 
varṇadāptyapapannaṃ hi maṇiratnaṃ praśasyate 
tābhyāmīṣadapi bhraṣṭaṃ maṇimūlyātprahīyate  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe padmarāgaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāma saptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
dānavādhipateḥ pittamādāya bhujagādhipaḥ 
dvidhā kurvanniva vyoma satvaraṃ vāsukiryayau  GarP 
sa tadā svaśiroratnaprabhādīpte nabho 'mbudhau 
rājataḥ samahānekaḥ khaṇḍaseturivābabhau  GarP 
tataḥ pakṣanipātena saṃharanniva rodasī 
garutmānpannagendrasya prahartumupacakrame  GarP 
sahasaiva mumoca tatphaṇīndraḥ surasābhyaktaturuṣka raṣka pādapāyām 
kalikāghanagandhavāsitā yāṃ varamāṇikyagirerupatyakāyām  GarP 
tasya prapātasamanantarakālameva tadvadvarālayamatītya ramāsamīpe 
sthānaṃ kṣiterupapayonidhitīralekhaṃyāṃ varamāṇikyagirerupatyakāyām  GarP 
tatraiva kiñcitpatatastu pittādupetya jagrāha tato garutmān 
mūrchāparītaḥ sahasaiva ghoṇārandhradvayena pramumoca sarvam  GarP 
tatrākaṭhoraśukakaṇṭhaśirīṣapuṣpakhadyotapṛṣṭhacaraśādvalaśaivalānām 
kalhāraśaṣpakabhujaṅgabhujāñca patraprāptatviṣo marakatāḥ śubhadā bhavanti  GarP 
tadyatra bhogīndrabhujābhiyuktaṃ papāta pittaṃ ditijādhipasya 
tasyākarasyātitarāṃ sa deśo duḥ khopalabhyaśca guṇaiśca yuktaḥ  GarP 
tasminmarakatasthāne yatkiñcidupajāyate 
tatsarvaṃ viṣarogāṇāṃ praśamāya prakīrtyate  GarP 
sarvamantrau ṣadhigaṇairyanna śakyaṃ cikitsitum 
mahāhidaṃṣṭrāprabhavaṃ viṣaṃ tattena śāmyati  GarP 
anyadapyākare tatra yaddoṣairupavarjitam 
jāyate tatpavitrāṇāmuttamaṃ parikīrtitam  GarP 
atyantaharitavarṇaṃ komalamarcirvibhedajaṭilaṃ ca 
kāñcanacūrṇasyāntaḥ pūrṇamiva lakṣyate yacca  GarP 
yuktaṃ saṃsthānaguṇaiḥ samarāgaṃ gauraveṇa na vihīnam 
savituḥ karasaṃsparśācchurayati sarvāśramaṃ dīptyā  GarP 
hitvā ca haritabhāvaṃ yasyāntarvinihitā bhaveddīptiḥ 
aciraprabhāprabhāhatanavaśādvalasannibhā bhāti  GarP 
yacca manasaḥ prasādaṃ vidadhāti nirīkṣyamatimātram 
nanmarakataṃ mahāgaṇamiti ratnavidāṃ manovṛttiḥ  GarP 
varṇasyāti vibhutvādyasyāntaḥ svacchakiraṇaparidhānam 
sāndrasnigdhaviśuddhaṃ komalabarhiprabhādisamakānti  GarP 
varṇojjvalayā kāntyā sāndrākāro vibhāsayā bhāti 
tadapi guṇavatsaṃjñāmāpnoti hi yādṛśī pūrvam  GarP 
śabalakaṭhoramalinaṃ rūkṣaṃ pāṣāṇakarkaropetam 
digdhaṃ śilājatunā marakatamevaṃvidhaṃ viguṇam  GarP 
yatsandhiśoṣitaṃ ratnamanyanmarakatādbhavet 
śreyaskāmairna taddhāryaṃ kretavyaṃ vā katañcana  GarP 
bhallātakī putrikā ca tadvarṇasamayogataḥ 
maṇermarakatasyaite lakṣaṇīyā vijātayaḥ  GarP 
kṣaumeṇa vāsasā mṛṣṭā dīptiṃ tyajati putrikā 
lāghavenaiva kācasya śakyā kartuṃ vibhāvanā  GarP 
kasyacidanekarūpairmarakatamanugacchato 'pi guṇavarṇaiḥ 
bhallātakasyasvanāttu vaiṣamyamupaiti varṇasya  GarP 
vajrāṇi muktāḥ santyanye ye ca keciddvijātayaḥ 
teṣāṃ nāpratibaddhānāṃ bhā bhavatyūrdhvagāminī  GarP 
ṛjutvāccaiva keṣāñcitkathañcidupajāyate 
tiryagālocyamānānāṃ sadyaścaiva praṇaśyati  GarP 
snānācamanajapyeṣu rakṣāmantrakriyāvidhau 
dadadbhirgohiraṇyāni kurvadbhiḥ sādhanāni ca  GarP 
daivapitryātitheyeṣu gurusaṃpūjaneṣu ca 
bādhyamāneṣu vividhairdeṣajātairviṣodbhavaiḥ  GarP 
dauṣairhenaṃ guṇairyuktaṃ kāñcanapratiyojitam 
saṃgrāme vicaradbhiśca dhāryaṃ marakataṃ budhaiḥ  GarP 
tulayā padmarāgasya yanmūlyamupajāyate 
labhate 'bhyadhikaṃ tasmādguṇairmarakataṃ yutam  GarP 
tathā ca padmarāgāṇāṃ doṣairmūlyaṃ prahīyate 
tato 'syāpyadhikā hānirdeṣairmarakate bhavet  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe purvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍa marakataparīkṣaṇaṃ nāmaikasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
tatraiva siṃhalavadhūkarapallavāgravyālūnabālalavalīkusumapravāle 
deśe papāta ditijasya nitāntakāntaṃ protphullanīrajasamadyuti netrayugmam  GarP 
tatpratyayādubhayaśobhanavīcibhāsā vistāriṇī jalanidherupakacchabhūmiḥ 
prodbhinnaketakavanapratibaddhalekhāsāndrendranīlamaṇiratnavatī vibhāti  GarP 
tatrāsitābjahalabhṛdvasanāsibhṛṅgaśārṅgāyudhāṅgaharakaṇṭhakaṣāyapuṣpaiḥ 
śuṣketaraiśca kusumairgirikarṇikāyāstasmādbhavanti maṇayaḥ sadṛśāvabhāsaḥ  GarP 
anye prasannapayasaḥ payasāṃ nidhāturambutviṣaḥ śikhigaṇapratimāstathānye 
nīlīrasaprabhavabudvudabhāśca kecitkecittathā samadakokilakaṇṭhabhāsaḥ  GarP 
ekaprakārā vispaṣṭavarṇaśobhāvabhāsinaḥ 
jāyante maṇayastasminnindranīlā mahāguṇāḥ  GarP 
mṛtpāṣāṇaśilārandhrakarkarātrāsasaṃyutāḥ 
abhrikāpaṭalacchāyāvarṇadoṣaiśca dūṣitāḥ  GarP 
tata eva hi jāyante maṇayastatra bhūrayaḥ 
sāstrasambodhitadhiyastānpraśaṃsanti sūrayaḥ  GarP 
dhāryamāṇasya ye dṛṣṭā padmarāgamaṇerguṇāḥ 
dhāraṇādindranīlasya tānevāpnoti mānavaḥ  GarP 
yathā ca padmarāgāṇāṃ jātakatritayaṃ bhavet 
indra nīleṣvapi tathā draṣṭavyamaviśeṣataḥ  GarP 
parīkṣāpratyayairyaiśca padmarāgaḥ parīkṣyate 
ta eva pratyayā dṛṣṭā indranīlamaṇerapi  GarP 
yāvantaṃ ca kramedagniṃ padmarāgopayogataḥ 
indranīlamaṇistasmātkrameta sumahattaram  GarP 
tathāpi na parīkṣārthaṃ guṇānāmabhi ti vṛddhaye 
maṇiragnau samādheyaḥ kathañcidapi kaścana  GarP 
agnimātrāparijñāne dāhadoṣaiśca dūpitaḥ 
so 'narthāya bhavedbhartuḥ kartuḥ kārayitustathā  GarP 
kācotpalakaravīrasphaṭikādyā iha budhaiḥ savaidūryāḥ 
kathitā vijātaya ime sadṛśā maṇinendranīlena  GarP 
gurubhāvakaṭhinabhāvāveteṣāṃ nityameva vijñeyau 
kācādyathāvaduttaravivardhamānau viśeṣeṇa  GarP 
indranīlo yathā kaścidvibhartyātāmravarṇatām 
rakṣaṇayau tathā tāmrau karavīrotpalāvubhau  GarP 
yasya madhyagatā bhāti nīlasyendrāyudhaprabhā 
tamindranīlamityāhurmahārhaṃ bhuvi durlabham  GarP 
yasya varṇasya bhūyastvātkṣīre śataguṇe sthitaḥ 
nīlatāṃ tannayetsarvaṃ mahānīlaḥ sa ucyate  GarP 
yatpadmarāgasya mahāguṇasya mūlyaṃ bhavenmāṣasamunmitasya 
tadindranīlasya mahāguṇasya suvarṇa saṃkhyātu litasya mūlyam  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe indranīlaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāma dvisaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
vaidūryapuṣparāgāṇāṃ karkete bhīṣmake vade 
parīkṣāṃ brahmaṇā proktāṃ vyāsena kathitāṃ dvijā  GarP 
kalpāntakālakṣubitāmburāśernirhrādakalpādditijasya nādāt 
vaidūryamutpannamanekavarṇaṃ śobhābhirāmadyutivarṇabījam  GarP 
avidūre vidūrasya gireruttuṅgarodhasaḥ 
kāmabhūtikasīmānamanu tasyākarobhavat  GarP 
tasya nādasamutthatvādākaraḥ sumahāguṇaḥ 
abhūduttarīto loke lokatrayavibhūṣaṇaḥ  GarP 
tasyaiva dānavapaterninadānurūpāḥ pravṛṭpayodavaradarśita cārurūpāḥ 
vaidūryaratnamaṇayo vividhāvabhāsastasmātsphuliṅganivahā iva saṃbabhūvuḥ  GarP 
padmarāgamupādāya maṇivarṇā hi ye kṣitau 
sarvāṃstānvarṇaśobhābhirvaidūryamanugacchati  GarP 
teṣāṃ pradhānaṃ śikhikaṇṭhanīlaṃ yadvā bhavedveṇudalaprakāśam 
cāṣāgrapakṣapratimaśriyo ye na te praśastā maṇiśāstravidbhiḥ  GarP 
guṇavānvaidūryamaṇiryojayati svāminaṃ paraṃbhā bho gyaiḥ 
doṣairyukto doṣaistasmādyatnātparīkṣeta  GarP 
girikācaśiśupālau kāca sphaṭikāśca dhūmanirbhinnāḥ 
vaidūryamaṇerete vijātayaḥ sannibhāḥ santi  GarP 
likhyābhāvātkācaṃ laghubhāvācchaisupālakaṃ vidyāt 
girikācasadīptitvātsphaṭikaṃ varṇojjvalatvena  GarP 
yadindranīlasya mahāguṇasya suvarṇasaṃkhyākalitasya mūlyam 
tadeva vaidūryamaṇeḥ pradiṣṭaṃ paladvayonmāpi tagauravasya  GarP 
jātyasya sarve 'pi maṇestu yādṛgvijātayaḥ santi samānavarṇāḥ 
tathāpi nānākaraṇānumeyabhedaprakāraḥ paramaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ  GarP 
sukhopalakṣyaśca sadā vicāryo hyayaṃ prabhedo viduṣā nareṇa 
snehaprabhedo laghutā mṛdutvaṃ vijātiliṅgaṃ khalu sārvajanyam  GarP 
kuśalākuśalaiḥ prapūryamāṇāḥ pratibaddhāḥ pratisatkriyāprayogaiḥ 
guṇadoṣasamudbhavaṃ labhante maṇayor'thontaramūlyameva bhinnāḥ  GarP 
kramaśaḥ samatītavartamānāḥ pratibaddhā maṇibandhakena yatnāt 
yadi nāma bhavanti doṣahīnā maṇayaḥ ṣaḍguṇamāpnuvanti mūlyam  GarP 
ākarānsamatītānāmudadhestīrasannidhau 
mūlyametanmaṇīnāṃ tu na sarvatra mahītale  GarP 
suvarṇo manunā yastu proktaḥ ṣoḍaśamāṣakaḥ 
tasya saptatimo bhāgaḥ saṃjñārūpaṃ kariṣyati  GarP 
śāṇaścaturmāṣamāno māṣakaḥ pañcakṛṣṇalaḥ 
palasya daśamo bhāgo dharaṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  GarP 
itthaṃ maṇividhiḥ prokto ratnānāṃ mūlyaniścaye  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe vaidūryaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāma trisaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca 
patitāyā himādrau tu tvacastasya suradviṣaḥ 
prādurbhavanti tābhyastu puṣpa ṣya
rāgā mahāguṇāḥ  GarP 
āpītapāṇḍuruciraḥ pāṣāṇaḥ padmarāgasaṃjñastu 
kaukaṇṭakanāmā syātsa eva yadi lohitāpītaḥ  GarP 
ālohitastu pītaḥ svacchaḥ kāṣāyakaḥ sa ekoktaḥ 
ānīlaśuklavarṇaḥ snigdhaḥ somālana
kaḥ saguṇaḥ  GarP 
atyantalohito yaḥ sa eva khalu padmarāgasaṃjñaḥ syāt 
api cendranīlasaṃjñaḥ sa eva kathitaḥ sunīlaḥ san  GarP 
mūlyaṃ vaidūryamaṇeriva gāditaṃ hyasya ratnasāravidā 
dhāraṇaphalaṃ ca tadvatkiṃ tu strīṇāṃ sutaprado bhavati  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe puṣparāgaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāma catuḥ saptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrīgaruḍamahāpurāṇam 
sūta uvāca 
vāyurnakhāndaityapatergṛhītvā cikṣepa satpadmavaneṣu hṛṣṭaḥ 
tataḥ prasūtaṃ pavanopapannaṃ karketanaṃ pūjayatamaṃ pṛthivyām  GarP 
varṇena tadrudhirasomamadhuprakāśamātāmrapītadahanojjvalitaṃ vibhāti 
nīlaṃ punaḥ khalu sitaṃ paruṣaṃ vibhinnaṃ vyādhyādidoṣakaraṇena ca tadvibhāti  GarP 
snigdhā viśuddhāḥ samarāgiṇaśca āpītavarṇā guravo vicitrāḥ 
trāsavraṇavyālavivarjitāśca karketanāste paramaṃ pavitrāḥ  GarP 
patreṇa kāñcanamayena tu veṣṭayitvā taptaṃ yadā hutavahe bhavati prakāśam 
rogapraṇāśanakaraṃ kalināśanaṃ tadāyuṣkaraṃ kulakaraṃ ca sukhapradaṃ ca  GarP 
evaṃvidhaṃ bahuguṇaṃ maṇimāvahanti karketanaṃ śubhalaṅkṛtaye narā ye 
te pūjitā bahudhanā bahubāndhavāśca nityojjvalāḥ pramuditā apite bhavanti  GarP 
eke 'panahya vikṛtākulanīlabhāsaḥ pramlānarāgalulitāḥ kaluṣā virūpāḥ 
tejo 'tidīpti kulapuṣṭivihīnavarṇāḥ karketanasya sadṛśaṃ vapurudvahanti  GarP 
karketanaṃ yadi parīkṣitavarṇarūpaṃ pratyagrabhāsvaradivākarasuprakāśam 
tasyottamasya maṇi śāstravidāṃ mahimnā tulyaṃ tu mūlyamuditaṃ tulitasya kāryam  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe karketanaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāma pañcasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca 
himavatyuttaradeśe vīryaṃ patitaṃ suradviṣastasya 
saṃprāptamuttamānāmākaratāṃ bhīṣmaratnānām  GarP 
śuklāḥ śaṅkhābjanibhāḥ syonākasannibhā prabhāvantaḥ 
prabhavanti tatastaruṇā vajranibhā bhīṣmapāṣāṇāḥ  GarP 
hemādipratibaddhāḥ śuddhamapi śraddhayā vidhatte yaḥ 
bhīṣmamaṇiṃ grīvādiṣu susampadaṃ sa sarvadā labhate  GarP 
nirīkṣya palāyante yaṃ tamaraṇyanivāsinaḥ samīpa'pi 
dvīpivṛkaśarabhakuñjarasiṃhavyāghrādayo hiṃstrāḥ  GarP 
tasoyatkalataṣṭatarorbhavati bhayaṃ na cāstīśamupahasanti 
bhīṣmamaṇirguṇayukto samyakprāptāṅgulīkalatratvaḥ  GarP 
pitṝtarpaṇe pitṝṇāṃ tṛptirbahuvārṣikī bhavati 
śāmyantyadbhutānyapi sarpāṇḍajākhuvṛścikaviṣāṇi 
salilāgnivairitaskarabhayāni bhīmāni naśyanti  GarP 
śaivalabalāhakābhaṃ puruṣaṃ pītaprabhaṃ prabhāhīnam 
malinadyuti ca vivarṇaṃ dūrātparivarjayetprājñaḥ  GarP 
mūlyaṃ prakalpyameṣāṃ vibudhavarairdaiśakālavijñānāt 
dūre bhūtānāṃ bahu kiñcinnikaṭaprasūtānām  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe vaidūryaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca 
puṇyeṣu parvatavareṣu ca nimnagāsu sthānāntareṣu ca tathottaradeśagatvāt 
saṃsthāpitāḥ svanakhabāhugateḥ prakāśaṃ saṃpūjya dānavapatiṃ prathite pradeśe  GarP 
dāśārṇavāgadara va
mekalakālagādau guñjāñjanakṣaudramṛṇālavarṇāḥ 
gandharvavahnikadalīsadṛśāvabhāsā ete praśastāḥ pulakāḥ prasūtāḥ  GarP 
śaṅkhābjabhṛṅgārkavicitrabhaṅgā sūtrairur vya
petāḥ paramāḥ pavitrāḥ 
maṅgalyayuktā bahubhakticitrā vṛddhipradāste pulakā bhavanti  GarP 
kākā kaśvarāsabhasṛgālavṛkograrūpairgṛdhraiḥ samāṃsarudhirārdramukhairupetāḥ 
mṛtyupradāśca viduṣā parivarjanīyā mūlyaṃ palasya kathitaṃ ca śatāni pañca  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe pulakaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāma saptasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca 
hutabhugrūpamādāya dānavasya yathepsitam

tatrendragopakalitaṃ śukavakravarṇaṃ saṃsthānataḥ prakaṭapīlusamānamātram 
nānāprakāravihitaṃ rudhirākṣakhya

sūta uvāca 
kāveravindhyayavanacīnanepālabhūmiṣu

iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe sphaṭikaparīkṣaṇaṃ nāmaikonāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca 
ādāya śeṣastasyāntraṃ balasya kelādiṣu 
cikṣepa tatra jāyante vidrumāḥ subhahāguṇāḥ  GarP 
tatra pradhānaṃ śaśalohitābhaṃ guñjājapāpuṣpanibhaṃ pradiṣṭam 
sunīlakaṃ devakaromakañca sthānāni teṣu prabhavaṃ surāgam  GarP 
anyatra jātaṃ ca na tatpradhānaṃ mūlyaṃ bhavecchilpiviśeṣayogāt 
prasannaṃ komalaṃ snigdhaṃ surāgaṃ vidrumaṃ hi tat  GarP 
dhanadhānyakaraṃ loke viṣārtibhayanāśanam

sphaṭikasya vidrumasya ratnajñānāya śaunaka   GarP

sūta uvāca 
sarvatīrthāni vakṣyāmi gaṅgā tīrthottamottamā 
sarvatra sulabhā gaṅgātriṣu sthāneṣu durlabhā  GarP 
gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame 
prayāgaṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ mṛtānāṃ bhuktimuktidam  GarP 
sevanātkṛtapiṇḍānāṃ pāpajitkāmadaṃ nṛṇām 
vārāṇasī paraṃ tīrthaṃ viśveśo yatra keśavaḥ  GarP 
kurukṣetraṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ dānādyairbhuktimuktidam 
prabhāsaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ somanātho hi tatra ca  GarP 
dvārakā ca purī ramyā bhuktimuktipradāyikā 
prācī sarasvatī puṇyā saptasārasvataṃ param  GarP 
kedāraṃ sarvapāpaghnaṃ sa śa
mbhalagrāma uttamaḥ 
naranarāyaṇaṃ tīrthaṃ muktyai vadarikāśramaḥ  GarP 
śvetadvīpaṃ purī māyā naimiṣaṃ puṣkaraṃ param 
ayodhyā cārghyatīrthaṃ tu citrakūṭaṃ ca gomatī  GarP 
vaināyakaṃ mahītīrthaṃ rāmagiryāśramaṃ param 
kāñcīpurī tuṅgabhadrā śrīśailaṃ setubandhanam  GarP 
rāmeśvaraṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ kārtikeyaṃ tathottamam 
bhṛgutuṅgaṃ kāmatīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ cāmarakaṇṭakam  GarP 
ujjayinyāṃ mahākālaḥ kubjake śrīdharo hariḥ 
kubjāmrakaṃ mahātīrthaṃ kālasarpiśca kāmadam  GarP 
mahā keśī ca kāverī candrabhāgā vipāśayā 
ekāmraṃ ca tathā tīrthaṃ brahmeśaṃ devakoṭakam  GarP 
mathurā ca purī ramyā śoṇaścaiva mahānadaḥ 
jambūsaro mahātīrthaṃ tāni tīrthāni viddhi ca  GarP 
sūryaḥ śivo gaṇo devī hariryatra ca tiṣṭhati 
eteṣu ca yathānyeṣu snānaṃ dānaṃ japastapaḥ  GarP 
pūjā śrāddhaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam 
śālagrāmaṃ sarvadaṃ syāttīrthaṃ paśupateḥ param  GarP 
kokāmukhaṃ ca vārāhaṃ bhā bhu
ṇḍīraṃ svāmisaṃjñakam 
lo mo hadaṇḍe mahāviṣṇurmandāre madhusūdanaḥ  GarP 
kāmarūpaṃ mahātīrthaṃ kāmākhyā kṣā
yatra tiṣṭhati 
puṇḍravardhanakaṃ tīrthaṃ kārtikeyaśca yatra ca  GarP 
virajastu mahātīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ śrīpuruṣottamam 
mahendraparvatastīrthaṃ kāverī ca nadī parā  GarP 
godāvarī mahātīrthaṃ payoṣṇī varadā nadī 
vindhyaḥ pāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ narmadābheda uttamaḥ  GarP 
gokarṇaṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ māhiṣmatī purī 
kālañjaraṃ mahītīrthaṃ śuklatīrthamanuttamam  GarP 
kṛte śauce muktidaṃ ca śārṅgadhārī tadantike 
virajaṃ sarvadaṃ tīrthaṃ svarṇākṣaṃ tīrthamuttamam  GarP 
nanditīrthaṃ muktidaṃ ca koṭitīrthaphalapradam 
nāsikyaṃ ca mahātīrthaṃ govardhanamataḥ param  GarP 
kṛṣṇaveṇī bhīmarathī gaṇḍakī yā tvirāvatī 
tīrthaṃ bindusaraḥ puṇyaṃ viṣṇupādodakaṃ param  GarP 
brahmadhyānaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ tīrthamindriyanigrahaḥ 
damastīrthaṃ tu paramaṃ bhavaśuddhiḥ paraṃ tathā  GarP 
jñānahrade dhyānajale rāgadveṣamalāpahe 
yaḥ snāti mānase tīrthe sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  GarP 
idaṃ tīrthamidaṃ neti ye narā bhedadarśinaḥ 
teṣāṃ vidhīyate tīrthagamanaṃ tatphalaṃ ca yat  GarP 
sarvaṃ brahmetiyo 'veti nātīrthaṃ tasya kiñcana 
eteṣu snānadānāni śrāddhaṃ piṇḍamathākṣayam  GarP 
sarvā nadyaḥ sarvaśailāḥ tīrthaṃ devādisevitam 
śrīraṅgaṃ ca harestīrthaṃ tāpī śreṣṭhā mahānadī  GarP 
saptagodāvaraṃ tīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ koṇagiriḥ param 
mahālakṣmīryatra devī praṇītā paramā nadī  GarP 
sahyādrau devadeveśa ekavīraḥ sureśvarī 
gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte vindhyake nīlaparvate  GarP 
snātvā kanakhale tīrthe sa bhavenna punarbhave 
sū uvāca 
etānyanyāni tīrthāni snānādyaiḥ sarvadāni hi  GarP 
śrutvābravīddharerbrahmā vyāsaṃ dakṣādisaṃyutam 
etānyuktvā ca tīrthāni puna stīrthottamottamam 
gayākhyaṃ prāha sarveṣāmakṣayaṃ brahmalokadam  GarP 
iti śrīgāruḍe mahāpurāṇe pūrvakhaṇḍe prathamāṃśākhye ācārakāṇḍe sarvatīrtha māhātmyaṃ nāmaikāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
